function dedup(xs: seq<int>): seq<int>
{
  if |xs| == 0 then []
  else if xs[0] in dedup(xs[1..]) then dedup(xs[1..])
  else [xs[0]] + dedup(xs[1..])
}

XP
function dedup(xs: seq<int>): seq<int>
{
  if |xs| == 0 then []
  else if xs[0] in dedup(xs[1..]) then dedup(xs[1..])
  else [xs[0]] + dedup(xs[1..])
}

predicate {:spec} noDuplicates(xs: seq<int>)
{
  forall i, j :: 0 <= i < j < |xs| ==> xs[i] != xs[j]
}

function {:spec} toSet(xs: seq<int>): set<int>
{
  set x | x in xs
}

lemma dedupCorrect(xs: seq<int>)
  ensures noDuplicates(dedup(xs))
  ensures toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(xs)
{
// For the base case: empty list
if xs == [] {
  // dedup([]) == [], so noDuplicates([]) holds trivially
  // toSet([]) == {} and toSet(dedup([])) == toSet([]) == {}
  assert noDuplicates(dedup([])) by {
    assert dedup([]) == [];
    assert noDuplicates([]);
  }
  assert toSet(dedup([])) == toSet([]) by {
    assert dedup([]) == [];
  }
}

// For non-empty list: xs = [x] + xs'
else {
  var x := xs[0];
  var xsTail := xs[1..];
  var dedupTail := dedup(xsTail);

  // Inductive hypothesis for the tail
  dedupCorrect(xsTail);

  // Now handle the main case
  if x in dedupTail {
    // Then dedup(xs) = dedupTail
    assert dedup(xs) == dedupTail by {
      assert xs == [x] + xsTail;
      assert dedup(xs) == if x in dedupTail then dedupTail else [x] + dedupTail;
    }
    // noDuplicates(dedupTail) holds by IH
    assert noDuplicates(dedup(xs)) by {
      assert dedup(xs) == dedupTail;
      assert noDuplicates(dedupTail) by dedupCorrect(xsTail);
    }
    // toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(dedupTail) == toSet(xsTail) by IH
    assert toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(xs) by {
      assert toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(dedupTail);
      assert toSet(dedupTail) == toSet(xsTail) by dedupCorrect(xsTail);
      assert toSet(xs) == toSet([x] + xsTail);
      assert toSet([x] + xsTail) == {x} + toSet(xsTail);
      assert x in dedupTail ==> {x} + toSet(xsTail) == toSet(xsTail);
      assert toSet(dedupTail) == toSet(xsTail);
    }
  } else {
    // Then dedup(xs) = [x] + dedupTail
    assert dedup(xs) == [x] + dedupTail by {
      assert xs == [x] + xsTail;
      assert dedup(xs) == if x in dedupTail then dedupTail else [x] + dedupTail;
    }
    // noDuplicates: need to show x not in dedupTail (already assumed) and dedupTail has no dups
    assert noDuplicates(dedup(xs)) by {
      assert dedup(xs) == [x] + dedupTail;
      assert noDuplicates([x] + dedupTail) by {
        // From IH: noDuplicates(dedupTail)
        assert noDuplicates(dedupTail);
        // From assumption: x !in dedupTail
        assert x !in dedupTail;
        // So appending x to front preserves no dups
      }
    }
    // toSet: {x} + toSet(dedupTail) == {x} + toSet(xsTail) == toSet([x] + xsTail) = toSet(xs)
    assert toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(xs) by {
      assert dedup(xs) == [x] + dedupTail;
      assert toSet([x] + dedupTail) == {x} + toSet(dedupTail);
      assert toSet(dedupTail) == toSet(xsTail) by dedupCorrect(xsTail);
      assert toSet(xs) == toSet([x] + xsTail) == {x} + toSet(xsTail);
    }
  }
}
}

function dedup(xs: seq<int>): seq<int>
{

  else [xs[0]] + dedup(xs[1..])

predicate {:spec} noDuplicates(xs: seq<int>)
{
  forall i, j :: 0 <= i < j < |xs| ==> xs[i] != xs[j]
}

function {:spec} toSet(xs: seq<int>): set<int>
{
  set x | x in xs
}

lemma dedupCorrect(xs: seq<int>)
  ensures noDuplicates(dedup(xs))
  ensures toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(xs)
{
if xs == [] {
  assert dedup([]) == [];
  assert noDuplicates(dedup([]));
  assert toSet(dedup([])) == toSet([]);
} else {
  var x := xs[0];
  var xsTail := xs[1..];
  var dedupTail := dedup(xsTail);

  dedupCorrect(xsTail);

  if x in dedupTail {
    assert dedup(xs) == dedupTail;
    assert noDuplicates(dedup(xs));
    assert toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(dedupTail);
    assert toSet(dedupTail) == toSet(xsTail);
    assert toSet(xs) == toSet([x] + xsTail);
    assert toSet([x] + xsTail) == {x} + toSet(xsTail);
    assert toSet(xs) == toSet(xsTail) by {
      assert x in dedupTail;
      assert toSet(dedupTail) == toSet(xsTail);
    }
    assert toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(xs);
  } else {
    assert dedup(xs) == [x] + dedupTail;
    assert noDuplicates([x] + dedupTail) by {
      assert noDuplicates(dedupTail);
      assert x !in dedupTail;
      assert forall i :: 0 <= i < |dedupTail| ==> x != dedupTail[i];
      assert forall i, j :: 0 <= i < j < |[x] + dedupTail| ==> ([x] + dedupTail)[i] != ([x] + dedupTail)[j];
    }
    assert noDuplicates(dedup(xs));
    assert toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet([x] + dedupTail);
    assert toSet([x] + dedupTail) == {x} + toSet(dedupTail);
    assert toSet(dedupTail) == toSet(xsTail);
    assert toSet(xs) == toSet([x] + xsTail);
    assert toSet([x] + xsTail) == {x} + toSet(xsTail);
    assert toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(xs);
  }
}
}

function dedup(xs: seq<int>): seq<int>
{
  if |xs| == 0 then []
  else if xs[0] in dedup(xs[1..]) then dedup(xs[1..])
  else [xs[0]] + dedup(xs[1..])
}

predicate {:spec} noDuplicates(xs: seq<int>)
{
  forall i, j :: 0 <= i < j < |xs| ==> xs[i] != xs[j]
}

function {:spec} toSet(xs: seq<int>): set<int>
{
  set x | x in xs
}

lemma dedupCorrect(xs: seq<int>)
  ensures noDuplicates(dedup(xs))
  ensures toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(xs)
{
if |xs| == 0 {
    // Base case: empty sequence
    // noDuplicates([]) holds vacuously
    // toSet([]) == {} == toSet([])
  } else {
    // Inductive step: non-empty sequence
    var tail := xs[1..];
    var dedupTail := dedup(tail);
    
    // By induction hypothesis for tail
    dedupCorrect(tail);
    
    // Now handle the head element xs[0]
    if xs[0] in dedupTail {
      // Case 1: head already in dedupTail
      // dedup(xs) == dedupTail
      // Since noDuplicates(dedupTail) and xs[0] is in dedupTail,
      // adding xs[0] would create duplicates, but we don't add it
      // so noDuplicates(dedup(xs)) holds
      // toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(dedupTail) == toSet(tail)
      // and toSet(xs) == {xs[0]} ∪ toSet(tail) == toSet(tail) since xs[0] ∈ dedupTail ⊆ toSet(tail)
      // Hence toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(xs)
    } else {
      // Case 2: head not in dedupTail
      // dedup(xs) == [xs[0]] + dedupTail
      // need to show: noDuplicates([xs[0]] + dedupTail)
      // by IH: noDuplicates(dedupTail) and xs[0] ∉ dedupTail
      // so noDuplicates holds
      // toSet([xs[0]] + dedupTail) == {xs[0]} ∪ toSet(dedupTail)
      // == {xs[0]} ∪ toSet(tail) == toSet(xs)
    }
  }
}

predicate {:spec} noDuplicates(xs: seq<int>)
{

{
  set x | x in xs

lemma dedupCorrect(xs: seq<int>)
  ensures noDuplicates(dedup(xs))
  ensures toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(xs)
{
if |xs| == 0 {
  // Base case: empty sequence
  // noDuplicates([]) holds vacuously
  // toSet([]) == {} == toSet([])
} else {
  // Inductive step: non-empty sequence
  var tail := xs[1..];
  var dedupTail := dedup(tail);
  
  // By induction hypothesis for tail
  dedupCorrect(tail);
  
  // Now handle the head element xs[0]
  if xs[0] in dedupTail {
    // Case 1: head already in dedupTail
    // dedup(xs) == dedupTail
    // noDuplicates(dedup(xs)) == noDuplicates(dedupTail) holds by IH
    // toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(dedupTail) == toSet(tail) by IH
    // toSet(xs) == {xs[0]} ∪ toSet(tail) == toSet(tail) since xs[0] in dedupTail ⊆ toSet(tail)
    // Hence toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(xs)
  } else {
    // Case 2: head not in dedupTail
    // dedup(xs) == [xs[0]] + dedupTail
    // noDuplicates([xs[0]] + dedupTail):
    // - By IH: noDuplicates(dedupTail)
    // - xs[0] ∉ dedupTail implies xs[0] ∉ {dedupTail[i] | 0 <= i < |dedupTail|}
    // - So first element differs from all others and inner elements are unique
    // toSet([xs[0]] + dedupTail) == {xs[0]} ∪ toSet(dedupTail)
    // == {xs[0]} ∪ toSet(tail) == toSet(xs) since toSet(xs) == {xs[0]} ∪ toSet(tail)
  }
}
}
XP
function dedup(xs: seq<int>): seq<int>
{
  if |xs| == 0 then []
  else if xs[0] in dedup(xs[1..]) then dedup(xs[1..])
  else [xs[0]] + dedup(xs[1..])
}

predicate {:spec} noDuplicates(xs: seq<int>)
{
  forall i, j :: 0 <= i < j < |xs| ==> xs[i] != xs[j]
}

function {:spec} toSet(xs: seq<int>): set<int>
{
  set x | x in xs
}

lemma dedupCorrect(xs: seq<int>)
  ensures noDuplicates(dedup(xs))
  ensures toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(xs)
{
if |xs| == 0 {
  // Base case: empty sequence
  // noDuplicates([]) holds vacuously
  // toSet([]) == {} == toSet([])
  assert noDuplicates([]);
  assert toSet([]) == toSet(xs);
} else {
  // Inductive step: non-empty sequence
  var tail := xs[1..];
  var dedupTail := dedup(tail);
  
  // By induction hypothesis for tail
  dedupCorrect(tail);
  
  // Now handle the head element xs[0]
  if xs[0] in dedupTail {
    // Case 1: head already in dedupTail
    // dedup(xs) == dedupTail
    assert dedup(xs) == dedupTail by {
      // By definition of dedup, when xs[0] in dedup(tail), dedup(xs) = dedup(tail)
      // This follows directly from the function definition
    };
    
    // noDuplicates(dedup(xs)) == noDuplicates(dedupTail) holds by IH
    assert noDuplicates(dedup(xs)) by {
      assert noDuplicates(dedupTail) by {
        dedupCorrect(tail);
      };
    };
    
    // toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(dedupTail) == toSet(tail) by IH
    assert toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(xs) by {
      assert toSet(dedupTail) == toSet(tail) by {
        dedupCorrect(tail);
      };
      // Since xs[0] in dedupTail, we have {xs[0]} ∪ toSet(tail) == toSet(tail)
      assert toSet(xs) == toSet(tail) by {
        // xs = [xs[0]] + tail, so toSet(xs) = {xs[0]} ∪ toSet(tail)
        // and xs[0] in toSet(tail) because xs[0] in dedupTail and toSet(dedupTail) == toSet(tail)
        assert xs[0] in toSet(tail);
      };
      assert toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(tail);
    };
  } else {
    // Case 2: head not in dedupTail
    // dedup(xs) == [xs[0]] + dedupTail
    assert dedup(xs) == [xs[0]] + dedupTail by {
      // By definition of dedup, when xs[0] !in dedup(tail), dedup(xs) = [xs[0]] + dedup(tail)
      // This follows directly from the function definition
    };
    
    // noDuplicates([xs[0]] + dedupTail):
    // - By IH: noDuplicates(dedupTail)
    // - xs[0] ∉ dedupTail implies xs[0] ∉ {dedupTail[i] | 0 <= i < |dedupTail|}
    // - So first element differs from all others and inner elements are unique
    assert noDuplicates([xs[0]] + dedupTail) by {
      // By induction hypothesis
      assert noDuplicates(dedupTail) by {
        dedupCorrect(tail);
      };
      // Show xs[0] is not in dedupTail
      assert xs[0] !in dedupTail;
      // Therefore, the concatenated sequence has no duplicates
      // We need to show: forall i, j :: 0 <= i < j < |[xs[0]] + dedupTail| ==> ([xs[0]] + dedupTail)[i] != ([xs[0]] + dedupTail)[j]
      // Case i=0, j>0: ([xs[0]] + dedupTail)[0] = xs[0], ([xs[0]] + dedupTail)[j] = dedupTail[j-1]
      // Since xs[0] !in dedupTail, xs[0] != dedupTail[j-1]
      // Case i>0, j>0: follows from noDuplicates(dedupTail)
    };
    
    // toSet([xs[0]] + dedupTail) == {xs[0]} ∪ toSet(dedupTail)
    // == {xs[0]} ∪ toSet(tail) == toSet(xs) since toSet(xs) == {xs[0]} ∪ toSet(tail)
    assert toSet(dedup(xs)) == toSet(xs) by {
      assert toSet([xs[0]] + dedupTail) == {xs[0]} + toSet(dedupTail) by {
        // Standard property of set conversion for sequences
      };
      assert toSet(dedupTail) == toSet(tail) by {
        dedupCorrect(tail);
      };
      // Since xs[0] !in dedupTail, we have xs[0] !in toSet(dedupTail), so
      // {xs[0]} ∪ toSet(dedupTail) is a disjoint union
      // And toSet(xs) = {xs[0]} ∪ toSet(tail), so equality follows
      assert toSet(xs) == {xs[0]} + toSet(tail) by {
        // xs = [xs[0]] + tail, so toSet(xs) = {xs[0]} ∪ toSet(tail)
      };
      assert {xs[0]} + toSet(dedupTail) == {xs[0]} + toSet(tail);
    };
  }
}
}

}

datatype Tree<T> = Leaf(value: T) | Node(left: Tree<T>, right: Tree<T>)

function flatten<T>(t: Tree<T>): seq<T>
{
  match t
  case Leaf(v) => [v]
  case Node(l, r) => flatten(l) + flatten(r)
}

function size<T>(t: Tree<T>): nat
{
  match t
  case Leaf(_) => 1
  case Node(l, r) => size(l) + size(r)
}

function toMultiset<T>(s: seq<T>): multiset<T>
{
  if |s| == 0 then multiset{}
  else multiset{s[0]} + toMultiset(s[1..])
}

function treeToMultiset<T>(t: Tree<T>): multiset<T>
{
  match t
  case Leaf(v) => multiset{v}
  case Node(l, r) => treeToMultiset(l) + treeToMultiset(r)
}

lemma toMultisetAppend<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures toMultiset(s1 + s2) == toMultiset(s1) + toMultiset(s2)
{
  if |s1| == 0 {
    assert s1 + s2 == s2;
  } else {
    toMultisetAppend(s1[1..], s2);
    assert s1 + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
  }
}

lemma flattenCorrect<T>(t: Tree<T>)
  ensures |flatten(t)| == size(t)
  ensures toMultiset(flatten(t)) == treeToMultiset(t)

datatype Tree<T> = Leaf(value: T) | Node(left: Tree<T>, right: Tree<T>)

function flatten<T>(t: Tree<T>): seq<T>
{
  match t
  case Leaf(v) => [v]
  case Node(l, r) => flatten(l) + flatten(r)
}

function size<T>(t: Tree<T>): nat
{
  match t
  case Leaf(_) => 1
  case Node(l, r) => size(l) + size(r)
}

function toMultiset<T>(s: seq<T>): multiset<T>
{
  if |s| == 0 then multiset{}
  else multiset{s[0]} + toMultiset(s[1..])
}

function treeToMultiset<T>(t: Tree<T>): multiset<T>
{
  match t
  case Leaf(v) => multiset{v}
  case Node(l, r) => treeToMultiset(l) + treeToMultiset(r)
}

lemma toMultisetAppend<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures toMultiset(s1 + s2) == toMultiset(s1) + toMultiset(s2)
{
  if |s1| == 0 {
    assert s1 + s2 == s2;
  } else {
    toMultisetAppend(s1[1..], s2);
    assert s1 + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
  }

lemma flattenCorrect<T>(t: Tree<T>)
  ensures |flatten(t)| == size(t)
  ensures toMultiset(flatten(t)) == treeToMultiset(t)
{
match t
case Leaf(v) =>
  assert |flatten(Leaf(v))| == |[v]| == 1 == size(Leaf(v));
  assert toMultiset(flatten(Leaf(v))) == toMultiset([v]) == multiset{v} == treeToMultiset(Leaf(v));
case Node(l, r) =>
  // Inductive hypothesis for left subtree
  flattenCorrect(l);
  // Inductive hypothesis for right subtree
  flattenCorrect(r);
  // Use IH to relate sizes and multisets
  assert |flatten(l)| == size(l);
  assert |flatten(r)| == size(r);
  assert |flatten(l) + flatten(r)| == |flatten(l)| + |flatten(r)| == size(l) + size(r) == size(Node(l, r));
  // For multiset part
  assert toMultiset(flatten(Node(l, r))) == toMultiset(flatten(l) + flatten(r));
  toMultisetAppend(flatten(l), flatten(r));
  assert toMultiset(flatten(l) + flatten(r)) == toMultiset(flatten(l)) + toMultiset(flatten(r));
  assert toMultiset(flatten(l)) == treeToMultiset(l) by {
    flattenCorrect(l);  // reuse IH for clarity (though already asserted above)
  }
  assert toMultiset(flatten(r)) == treeToMultiset(r) by {
    flattenCorrect(r);
  }
  assert toMultiset(flatten(Node(l, r))) == treeToMultiset(l) + treeToMultiset(r) == treeToMultiset(Node(l, r));
}

datatype Tree<T> = Leaf(value: T) | Node(left: Tree<T>, right: Tree<T>)

function flatten<T>(t: Tree<T>): seq<T>
{
  match t
  case Leaf(v) => [v]
  case Node(l, r) => flatten(l) + flatten(r)
}

function size<T>(t: Tree<T>): nat
{
  match t
  case Leaf(_) => 1
  case Node(l, r) => size(l) + size(r)
}

function toMultiset<T>(s: seq<T>): multiset<T>
{
  if |s| == 0 then multiset{}
  else multiset{s[0]} + toMultiset(s[1..])
}

function treeToMultiset<T>(t: Tree<T>): multiset<T>
{
  match t
  case Leaf(v) => multiset{v}
  case Node(l, r) => treeToMultiset(l) + treeToMultiset(r)
}

lemma toMultisetAppend<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures toMultiset(s1 + s2) == toMultiset(s1) + toMultiset(s2)
{
  if |s1| == 0 {
    assert s1 + s2 == s2;
  } else {
    toMultisetAppend(s1[1..], s2);
    assert s1 + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
  }
}

  ensures |flatten(t)| == size(t)
  ensures toMultiset(flatten(t)) == treeToMultiset(t)
{
  match t
  case Leaf(v) => {
}
  case Node(l, r) => {
}
}

datatype Tree<T> = Leaf(value: T) | Node(left: Tree<T>, right: Tree<T>)

function flatten<T>(t: Tree<T>): seq<T>
{
  match t
  case Leaf(v) => [v]
  case Node(l, r) => flatten(l) + flatten(r)
}

function size<T>(t: Tree<T>): nat
{
  match t
  case Leaf(_) => 1
  case Node(l, r) => size(l) + size(r)
}

function toMultiset<T>(s: seq<T>): multiset<T>
{
  if |s| == 0 then multiset{}
  else multiset{s[0]} + toMultiset(s[1..])
}

function treeToMultiset<T>(t: Tree<T>): multiset<T>
{
  match t
  case Leaf(v) => multiset{v}
  case Node(l, r) => treeToMultiset(l) + treeToMultiset(r)
}

lemma toMultisetAppend<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures toMultiset(s1 + s2) == toMultiset(s1) + toMultiset(s2)
{
  if |s1| == 0 {
    assert s1 + s2 == s2;
  } else {
    toMultisetAppend(s1[1..], s2);
    assert s1 + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
  }
}

lemma flattenCorrect<T>(t: Tree<T>)
  ensures |flatten(t)| == size(t)
  ensures toMultiset(flatten(t)) == treeToMultiset(t)
{
match t
case Leaf(v) => {
  // For Leaf: flatten(t) = [v], so |flatten(t)| = 1 = size(t)
  // and toMultiset(flatten(t)) = toMultiset([v]) = multiset{v} = treeToMultiset(t)
  assert |[v]| == 1;
  assert toMultiset([v]) == multiset{v};
}
case Node(l, r) => {
  // Induction hypothesis for left and right subtrees
  flattenCorrect(l);
  flattenCorrect(r);
  
  // First postcondition: |flatten(t)| == size(t)
  // By definition: |flatten(t)| = |flatten(l) + flatten(r)|
  // = |flatten(l)| + |flatten(r)| (by seq length property)
  // = size(l) + size(r) (by IH)
  // = size(t)
  assert |flatten(l) + flatten(r)| == |flatten(l)| + |flatten(r)|;
  assert |flatten(l)| == size(l) by { assert flattenCorrect(l); }
  assert |flatten(r)| == size(r) by { assert flattenCorrect(r); }
  assert |flatten(t)| == size(l) + size(r);
  assert size(t) == size(l) + size(r);
  
  // Second postcondition: toMultiset(flatten(t)) == treeToMultiset(t)
  // By definition: toMultiset(flatten(t)) = toMultiset(flatten(l) + flatten(r))
  // = toMultiset(flatten(l)) + toMultiset(flatten(r)) (by toMultisetAppend)
  // = treeToMultiset(l) + treeToMultiset(r) (by IH)
  // = treeToMultiset(t)
  toMultisetAppend(flatten(l), flatten(r));
  assert toMultiset(flatten(l)) == treeToMultiset(l) by { assert flattenCorrect(l); }
  assert toMultiset(flatten(r)) == treeToMultiset(r) by { assert flattenCorrect(r); }
  assert treeToMultiset(t) == treeToMultiset(l) + treeToMultiset(r);
}
}
XP
datatype Tree<T> = Leaf(value: T) | Node(left: Tree<T>, right: Tree<T>)

function flatten<T>(t: Tree<T>): seq<T>
{
  match t
  case Leaf(v) => [v]
  case Node(l, r) => flatten(l) + flatten(r)
}

function size<T>(t: Tree<T>): nat
{
  match t
  case Leaf(_) => 1
  case Node(l, r) => size(l) + size(r)
}

function toMultiset<T>(s: seq<T>): multiset<T>
{
  if |s| == 0 then multiset{}
  else multiset{s[0]} + toMultiset(s[1..])
}

function treeToMultiset<T>(t: Tree<T>): multiset<T>
{
  match t
  case Leaf(v) => multiset{v}
  case Node(l, r) => treeToMultiset(l) + treeToMultiset(r)
}

lemma toMultisetAppend<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures toMultiset(s1 + s2) == toMultiset(s1) + toMultiset(s2)
{
  if |s1| == 0 {
    assert s1 + s2 == s2;
  } else {
    toMultisetAppend(s1[1..], s2);
    assert s1 + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
  }
}

lemma flattenCorrect<T>(t: Tree<T>)
  ensures |flatten(t)| == size(t)
  ensures toMultiset(flatten(t)) == treeToMultiset(t)
{
match t
case Leaf(v) => {
  assert |[v]| == 1 by {
    assert [v].Length == 1;
  }
  assert toMultiset([v]) == multiset{v} by {
    assert toMultiset([v]) == multiset{v} by {
      // base case for toMultiset
    }
  }
}
case Node(l, r) => {
  // Recursive calls establish induction hypotheses
  flattenCorrect(l);
  flattenCorrect(r);
  
  // First postcondition: length equality
  assert |flatten(t)| == |flatten(l) + flatten(r)| by {
    assert flatten(t) == flatten(l) + flatten(r);
  }
  assert |flatten(l) + flatten(r)| == |flatten(l)| + |flatten(r)| by {
    assert (flatten(l) + flatten(r)).Length == flatten(l).Length + flatten(r).Length;
  }
  assert |flatten(l)| == size(l) by {
    // from flattenCorrect(l) postcondition
  }
  assert |flatten(r)| == size(r) by {
    // from flattenCorrect(r) postcondition
  }
  assert |flatten(l)| + |flatten(r)| == size(l) + size(r) by {
    // arithmetic
  }
  assert size(t) == size(l) + size(r) by {
    assert size(t) == size(l) + size(r);
  }
  
  // Second postcondition: multiset equality
  toMultisetAppend(flatten(l), flatten(r));
  assert toMultiset(flatten(t)) == toMultiset(flatten(l)) + toMultiset(flatten(r)) by {
    // from toMultisetAppend
  }
  assert toMultiset(flatten(l)) == treeToMultiset(l) by {
    // from flattenCorrect(l) postcondition
  }
  assert toMultiset(flatten(r)) == treeToMultiset(r) by {
    // from flattenCorrect(r) postcondition
  }
  assert treeToMultiset(t) == treeToMultiset(l) + treeToMultiset(r) by {
    assert treeToMultiset(t) == treeToMultiset(l) + treeToMultiset(r);
  }
}
}

datatype Tree<T> = Leaf(value: T) | Node(left: Tree<T>, right: Tree<T>)

function flatten<T>(t: Tree<T>): seq<T>
{
  match t
  case Leaf(v) => [v]
  case Node(l, r) => flatten(l) + flatten(r)
}

function size<T>(t: Tree<T>): nat
{
  match t
  case Leaf(_) => 1
  case Node(l, r) => size(l) + size(r)
}

function toMultiset<T>(s: seq<T>): multiset<T>
{
  if |s| == 0 then multiset{}
  else multiset{s[0]} + toMultiset(s[1..])
}

function treeToMultiset<T>(t: Tree<T>): multiset<T>
{
  match t
  case Leaf(v) => multiset{v}
  case Node(l, r) => treeToMultiset(l) + treeToMultiset(r)
}

lemma toMultisetAppend<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures toMultiset(s1 + s2) == toMultiset(s1) + toMultiset(s2)
{
  if |s1| == 0 {
    assert s1 + s2 == s2;
  } else {
    toMultisetAppend(s1[1..], s2);
    assert s1 + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
  }
}

lemma flattenCorrect<T>(t: Tree<T>)
  ensures |flatten(t)| == size(t)
  ensures toMultiset(flatten(t)) == treeToMultiset(t)
{
match t
case Leaf(v) => {
  assert |flatten(t)| == size(t) by {
    assert |[v]| == 1;
  }
  assert toMultiset(flatten(t)) == treeToMultiset(t) by {
    assert toMultiset([v]) == multiset{v};
  }
}
case Node(l, r) => {
  flattenCorrect(l);
  flattenCorrect(r);
  
  // First postcondition: length equality
  assert |flatten(t)| == size(t) by {
    assert flatten(t) == flatten(l) + flatten(r);
    assert |flatten(l) + flatten(r)| == |flatten(l)| + |flatten(r)|;
    assert |flatten(l)| == size(l);
    assert |flatten(r)| == size(r);
    assert size(t) == size(l) + size(r);
  }
  
  // Second postcondition: multiset equality
  toMultisetAppend(flatten(l), flatten(r));
  assert toMultiset(flatten(t)) == toMultiset(flatten(l)) + toMultiset(flatten(r));
  assert toMultiset(flatten(l)) == treeToMultiset(l);
  assert toMultiset(flatten(r)) == treeToMultiset(r);
  assert treeToMultiset(t) == treeToMultiset(l) + treeToMultiset(r);
  assert toMultiset(flatten(t)) == treeToMultiset(t);
}
}

// Min-heap operations: insert, extractMin, heapify with heap property

datatype Heap = Heap(elements: seq<int>)

// Check if heap is empty
predicate {:spec} heapIsEmpty(h: Heap)
{
  |h.elements| == 0
}

// Get heap size
function {:spec} heapSize(h: Heap): nat
{
  |h.elements|
}

// Parent index in heap
function {:spec} parent(i: nat): nat
  requires i > 0
{
  (i - 1) / 2
}

// Left child index
function {:spec} leftChild(i: nat): nat
{
  2 * i + 1
}

// Right child index
function {:spec} rightChild(i: nat): nat
{
  2 * i + 2
}

// Check min-heap property
predicate {:spec} isMinHeap(h: Heap)
{
  forall i :: 0 < i < |h.elements| ==> h.elements[parent(i)] <= h.elements[i]
}

// Check max-heap property
predicate {:spec} isMaxHeap(h: Heap)
{
  forall i :: 0 < i < |h.elements| ==> h.elements[parent(i)] >= h.elements[i]
}

// Get minimum element (root of min-heap)
function {:spec} getMin(h: Heap): int
  requires !heapIsEmpty(h)
  requires isMinHeap(h)
{
  h.elements[0]
}

// Get maximum element (root of max-heap)
function {:spec} getMax(h: Heap): int
  requires !heapIsEmpty(h)
  requires isMaxHeap(h)
{
  h.elements[0]
}

// Check if element exists in heap
predicate {:spec} heapContains(h: Heap, x: int)
{
  x in h.elements
}

// Create empty heap
function {:spec} emptyHeap(): Heap
{
  Heap([])
}

// Create heap from single element
function {:spec} singletonHeap(x: int): Heap
{
  Heap([x])
}

// Swap two elements in sequence
function {:spec} swap(s: seq<int>, i: nat, j: nat): seq<int>
  requires i < |s| && j < |s|
{
  s[i := s[j]][j := s[i]]
}

// Check if heap is complete binary tree (always true for array representation)
predicate {:spec} isComplete(h: Heap)
{
  true  // Array representation is always complete
}

// Get height of heap
function {:spec} heapHeight(h: Heap): nat
{
  if |h.elements| == 0 then 0
  else log2Floor(|h.elements|) + 1
}

// Floor of log base 2
function {:spec} log2Floor(n: nat): nat
  requires n > 0
  decreases n
{
  if n == 1 then 0
  else 1 + log2Floor(n / 2)
}

// Check if index is valid
predicate {:spec} validIndex(h: Heap, i: nat)
{
  i < |h.elements|
}

// Get all elements at a given level
function {:spec} getLevel(h: Heap, level: nat): seq<int>
{
  getLevelHelper(h, level, 0)
}

function getLevelHelper(h: Heap, targetLevel: nat, currentLevel: nat): seq<int>
  decreases |h.elements| - currentLevel
{
  if currentLevel >= |h.elements| || currentLevel >= Power2(targetLevel) then []
  else if currentLevel >= Power2(targetLevel) - 1 && currentLevel < Power2(targetLevel + 1) - 1 then
    if currentLevel < |h.elements| then [h.elements[currentLevel]] + getLevelHelper(h, targetLevel, currentLevel + 1)
    else []
  else getLevelHelper(h, targetLevel, currentLevel + 1)
}

function Power2(n: nat): nat
{
  if n == 0 then 1
  else 2 * Power2(n - 1)
}

// --- Lemmas for correctness ---

lemma EmptyHeapIsMinHeap()
  ensures isMinHeap(emptyHeap())
{
  var h := emptyHeap();
  forall i | 0 < i < |h.elements|
    ensures h.elements[parent(i)] <= h.elements[i]
  {
    assert false;  // No such i exists
  }
}

lemma EmptyHeapIsMaxHeap()
  ensures isMaxHeap(emptyHeap())
{
  var h := emptyHeap();
  forall i | 0 < i < |h.elements|
    ensures h.elements[parent(i)] >= h.elements[i]
  {
    assert false;  // No such i exists
  }
}

lemma SingletonIsMinHeap(x: int)
  ensures isMinHeap(singletonHeap(x))
{
  var h := singletonHeap(x);
  forall i | 0 < i < |h.elements|
    ensures h.elements[parent(i)] <= h.elements[i]
  {
    assert false;  // No such i exists since |h.elements| == 1
  }
}

lemma SingletonIsMaxHeap(x: int)
  ensures isMaxHeap(singletonHeap(x))
{
  var h := singletonHeap(x);
  forall i | 0 < i < |h.elements|
    ensures h.elements[parent(i)] >= h.elements[i]
  {
    assert false;  // No such i exists since |h.elements| == 1
  }
}

lemma MinHeapRootIsMinimum(h: Heap)
  requires !heapIsEmpty(h)
  requires isMinHeap(h)
  ensures forall i :: 0 <= i < |h.elements| ==> h.elements[0] <= h.elements[i]
{
  if |h.elements| == 1 {
    forall i | 0 <= i < |h.elements|
      ensures h.elements[0] <= h.elements[i]
    {
      assert i == 0;
    }
  } else {
    forall i | 0 <= i < |h.elements|
      ensures h.elements[0] <= h.elements[i]
    {
      if i == 0 {
        // Trivial
      } else {
        MinHeapPathToRoot(h, i);
      }
    }
  }
}

lemma MinHeapPathToRoot(h: Heap, i: nat)
  requires isMinHeap(h)
  requires 0 < i < |h.elements|
  ensures h.elements[0] <= h.elements[i]
{
  if parent(i) == 0 {
    assert h.elements[0] <= h.elements[i];
  } else {
    assert h.elements[parent(i)] <= h.elements[i];
    MinHeapPathToRoot(h, parent(i));
  }
}

lemma MaxHeapRootIsMaximum(h: Heap)
  requires !heapIsEmpty(h)
  requires isMaxHeap(h)
  ensures forall i :: 0 <= i < |h.elements| ==> h.elements[0] >= h.elements[i]
{
  if |h.elements| == 1 {
    forall i | 0 <= i < |h.elements|
      ensures h.elements[0] >= h.elements[i]
    {
      assert i == 0;
    }
  } else {
    forall i | 0 <= i < |h.elements|
      ensures h.elements[0] >= h.elements[i]
    {
      if i == 0 {
        // Trivial
      } else {
        MaxHeapPathToRoot(h, i);
      }
    }
  }
}

lemma MaxHeapPathToRoot(h: Heap, i: nat)
  requires isMaxHeap(h)
  requires 0 < i < |h.elements|
  ensures h.elements[0] >= h.elements[i]
{
  if parent(i) == 0 {
    assert h.elements[0] >= h.elements[i];
  } else {
    assert h.elements[parent(i)] >= h.elements[i];
    MaxHeapPathToRoot(h, parent(i));
  }
}

lemma ParentChildRelation(i: nat)
  requires i > 0
  ensures leftChild(parent(i)) == i || rightChild(parent(i)) == i
  ensures leftChild(parent(i)) == i <==> i % 2 == 1
  ensures rightChild(parent(i)) == i <==> i % 2 == 0
{
  var p := parent(i);
  assert p == (i - 1) / 2;
  assert leftChild(p) == 2 * p + 1;
  assert rightChild(p) == 2 * p + 2;

  if i % 2 == 1 {
    assert i == 2 * ((i - 1) / 2) + 1;
    assert leftChild(p) == i;
  } else {
    assert i % 2 == 0;
    assert i == 2 * ((i - 1) / 2) + 2;
    assert rightChild(p) == i;
  }
}

lemma HeapHeightBound(h: Heap)
  ensures heapHeight(h) <= |h.elements|
{

}

lemma Log2FloorBound(n: nat)
  requires n > 0
  ensures log2Floor(n) < n
  decreases n
{
  if n == 1 {
    assert log2Floor(1) == 0;
  } else {
    Log2FloorBound(n / 2);
    assert log2Floor(n) == 1 + log2Floor(n / 2);
    assert n / 2 < n;
  }
}

lemma SwapPreservesMultiset(s: seq<int>, i: nat, j: nat)
  requires i < |s| && j < |s|
  ensures multiset(swap(s, i, j)) == multiset(s)
{
  var s' := swap(s, i, j);
  assert s'[i] == s[j];
  assert s'[j] == s[i];
  forall k | 0 <= k < |s| && k != i && k != j
    ensures s'[k] == s[k]
  {
    // Elements other than i and j are unchanged
  }
}

  ensures isMaxHeap(emptyHeap())
{

  forall i | 0 < i < |h.elements|
    ensures h.elements[parent(i)] >= h.elements[i]

lemma MinHeapRootIsMinimum(h: Heap)
  requires !heapIsEmpty(h)
  requires isMinHeap(h)
  ensures forall i :: 0 <= i < |h.elements| ==> h.elements[0] <= h.elements[i]
{
  if |h.elements| == 1 {
    forall i | 0 <= i < |h.elements|
      ensures h.elements[0] <= h.elements[i]
    {
      assert i == 0;
    }
  } else {
    forall i | 0 <= i < |h.elements|
      ensures h.elements[0] <= h.elements[i]
    {
      if i == 0 {
        // Trivial
      } else {
        MinHeapPathToRoot(h, i);
      }
    }
  }
}

lemma MinHeapPathToRoot(h: Heap, i: nat)
  requires isMinHeap(h)
  requires 0 < i < |h.elements|
  ensures h.elements[0] <= h.elements[i]
{
  if parent(i) == 0 {
    assert h.elements[0] <= h.elements[i];
  } else {
    assert h.elements[parent(i)] <= h.elements[i];
    MinHeapPathToRoot(h, parent(i));
  }
}

lemma MaxHeapRootIsMaximum(h: Heap)
  requires !heapIsEmpty(h)
  requires isMaxHeap(h)
  ensures forall i :: 0 <= i < |h.elements| ==> h.elements[0] >= h.elements[i]
{
  if |h.elements| == 1 {
    forall i | 0 <= i < |h.elements|
      ensures h.elements[0] >= h.elements[i]
    {
      assert i == 0;
    }
  } else {
    forall i | 0 <= i < |h.elements|
      ensures h.elements[0] >= h.elements[i]
    {
      if i == 0 {
        // Trivial
      } else {
        MaxHeapPathToRoot(h, i);
      }
    }
  }
}

lemma MaxHeapPathToRoot(h: Heap, i: nat)
  requires isMaxHeap(h)
  requires 0 < i < |h.elements|
  ensures h.elements[0] >= h.elements[i]
{
  if parent(i) == 0 {
    assert h.elements[0] >= h.elements[i];
  } else {
    assert h.elements[parent(i)] >= h.elements[i];
    MaxHeapPathToRoot(h, parent(i));
  }
}

lemma ParentChildRelation(i: nat)
  requires i > 0
  ensures leftChild(parent(i)) == i || rightChild(parent(i)) == i
  ensures leftChild(parent(i)) == i <==> i % 2 == 1
  ensures rightChild(parent(i)) == i <==> i % 2 == 0
{
  var p := parent(i);
  assert p == (i - 1) / 2;
  assert leftChild(p) == 2 * p + 1;
  assert rightChild(p) == 2 * p + 2;

  if i % 2 == 1 {
    assert i == 2 * ((i - 1) / 2) + 1;
    assert leftChild(p) == i;
  } else {
    assert i % 2 == 0;
    assert i == 2 * ((i - 1) / 2) + 2;
    assert rightChild(p) == i;
  }
}

lemma HeapHeightBound(h: Heap)
  ensures heapHeight(h) <= |h.elements|
{

}

lemma Log2FloorBound(n: nat)
  requires n > 0
  ensures log2Floor(n) < n
  decreases n
{
  if n == 1 {
    assert log2Floor(1) == 0;
  } else {
    Log2FloorBound(n / 2);
    assert log2Floor(n) == 1 + log2Floor(n / 2);
    assert n / 2 < n;
  }
}

lemma SwapPreservesMultiset(s: seq<int>, i: nat, j: nat)
  requires i < |s| && j < |s|
  ensures multiset(swap(s, i, j)) == multiset(s)
{
  var s' := swap(s, i, j);
  assert s'[i] == s[j];
  assert s'[j] == s[i];
  forall k | 0 <= k < |s| && k != i && k != j
    ensures s'[k] == s[k]
  {
    // Elements other than i and j are unchanged
  }
}

// Min-heap operations: insert, extractMin, heapify with heap property

datatype Heap = Heap(elements: seq<int>)

// Check if heap is empty
predicate {:spec} heapIsEmpty(h: Heap)
{
  |h.elements| == 0
}

// Get heap size
function {:spec} heapSize(h: Heap): nat
{
  |h.elements|
}

// Parent index in heap
function {:spec} parent(i: nat): nat
  requires i > 0
{
  (i - 1) / 2
}

// Left child index
function {:spec} leftChild(i: nat): nat
{
  2 * i + 1
}

// Right child index
function {:spec} rightChild(i: nat): nat
{
  2 * i + 2
}

// Check min-heap property
predicate {:spec} isMinHeap(h: Heap)
{
  forall i :: 0 < i < |h.elements| ==> h.elements[parent(i)] <= h.elements[i]
}

// Check max-heap property
predicate {:spec} isMaxHeap(h: Heap)
{
  forall i :: 0 < i < |h.elements| ==> h.elements[parent(i)] >= h.elements[i]
}

// Get minimum element (root of min-heap)
function {:spec} getMin(h: Heap): int
  requires !heapIsEmpty(h)
  requires isMinHeap(h)
{
  h.elements[0]
}

// Get maximum element (root of max-heap)
function {:spec} getMax(h: Heap): int
  requires !heapIsEmpty(h)
  requires isMaxHeap(h)
{
  h.elements[0]
}

// Check if element exists in heap
predicate {:spec} heapContains(h: Heap, x: int)
{
  x in h.elements
}

// Create empty heap
function {:spec} emptyHeap(): Heap
{
  Heap([])
}

// Create heap from single element
function {:spec} singletonHeap(x: int): Heap
{
  Heap([x])
}

// Swap two elements in sequence
function {:spec} swap(s: seq<int>, i: nat, j: nat): seq<int>
  requires i < |s| && j < |s|
{
  s[i := s[j]][j := s[i]]
}

// Check if heap is complete binary tree (always true for array representation)
predicate {:spec} isComplete(h: Heap)
{
  true  // Array representation is always complete
}

// Get height of heap
function {:spec} heapHeight(h: Heap): nat
{
  if |h.elements| == 0 then 0
  else log2Floor(|h.elements|) + 1
}

// Floor of log base 2
function {:spec} log2Floor(n: nat): nat
  requires n > 0
  decreases n
{
  if n == 1 then 0
  else 1 + log2Floor(n / 2)
}

// Check if index is valid
predicate {:spec} validIndex(h: Heap, i: nat)
{
  i < |h.elements|
}

// Get all elements at a given level
function {:spec} getLevel(h: Heap, level: nat): seq<int>
{
  getLevelHelper(h, level, 0)
}

function getLevelHelper(h: Heap, targetLevel: nat, currentLevel: nat): seq<int>
  decreases |h.elements| - currentLevel
{
  if currentLevel >= |h.elements| || currentLevel >= Power2(targetLevel) then []
  else if currentLevel >= Power2(targetLevel) - 1 && currentLevel < Power2(targetLevel + 1) - 1 then
    if currentLevel < |h.elements| then [h.elements[currentLevel]] + getLevelHelper(h, targetLevel, currentLevel + 1)
    else []
  else getLevelHelper(h, targetLevel, currentLevel + 1)
}

function Power2(n: nat): nat
{
  if n == 0 then 1
  else 2 * Power2(n - 1)
}

// --- Lemmas for correctness ---

    ensures h.elements[parent(i)] <= h.elements[i]

  }

lemma ParentChildRelation(i: nat)
  requires i > 0
  ensures leftChild(parent(i)) == i || rightChild(parent(i)) == i
  ensures leftChild(parent(i)) == i <==> i % 2 == 1
  ensures rightChild(parent(i)) == i <==> i % 2 == 0
{
  var p := parent(i);
  assert p == (i - 1) / 2;
  assert leftChild(p) == 2 * p + 1;
  assert rightChild(p) == 2 * p + 2;

  if i % 2 == 1 {
    assert i == 2 * ((i - 1) / 2) + 1;
    assert leftChild(p) == i;
  } else {
    assert i % 2 == 0;
    assert i == 2 * ((i - 1) / 2) + 2;
    assert rightChild(p) == i;
  }
}

lemma HeapHeightBound(h: Heap)
  ensures heapHeight(h) <= |h.elements|
{
var n := |h.elements|;
if n == 0 {
  assert heapHeight(h) == 0;
  assert 0 <= 0;
} else {
  assert heapHeight(h) == log2Floor(n) + 1;
  // Prove log2Floor(n) + 1 <= n for all n > 0
  // Base case: n = 1
  // log2Floor(1) = 0, so 0 + 1 = 1 <= 1 ✓
  // Inductive step: assume true for all m < n, prove for n > 1
  // Since n > 1, log2Floor(n) = 1 + log2Floor(n/2)
  // By induction hypothesis: log2Floor(n/2) < n/2
  // So log2Floor(n) + 1 = 1 + log2Floor(n/2) + 1 = log2Floor(n/2) + 2
  // Need to show: log2Floor(n/2) + 2 <= n
  // Since n > 1, n >= 2, so n/2 >= 1
  // By Log2FloorBound(n): log2Floor(n/2) < n/2
  // So log2Floor(n/2) + 2 < n/2 + 2
  // For n >= 2: n/2 + 2 <= n  ⇔  2 <= n/2  ⇔  n >= 4
  // For n = 2: log2Floor(2) + 1 = 1 + 1 = 2 <= 2 ✓
  // For n = 3: log2Floor(3) + 1 = 1 + 1 = 2 <= 3 ✓
  // So in all cases: log2Floor(n) + 1 <= n
  if n == 1 {
    assert log2Floor(1) + 1 == 1;
  } else if n == 2 {
    assert log2Floor(2) + 1 == 2;
  } else if n == 3 {
    assert log2Floor(3) + 1 == 2;
  } else {
    // n >= 4
    Log2FloorBound(n);
    assert log2Floor(n) < n;
    assert log2Floor(n) + 1 <= n;
  }
}
}

lemma Log2FloorBound(n: nat)
  requires n > 0
  ensures log2Floor(n) < n
  decreases n
{
  if n == 1 {
    assert log2Floor(1) == 0;
  } else {
    Log2FloorBound(n / 2);
    assert log2Floor(n) == 1 + log2Floor(n / 2);
    assert n / 2 < n;
  }
}

  assert s'[j] == s[i];
  forall k | 0 <= k < |s| && k != i && k != j
    ensures s'[k] == s[k]
  {
    // Elements other than i and j are unchanged
  }
}

  decreases |h.elements| - currentLevel
{
  if currentLevel >= |h.elements| || currentLevel >= Power2(targetLevel) then []
  else if currentLevel >= Power2(targetLevel) - 1 && currentLevel < Power2(targetLevel + 1) - 1 then
    if currentLevel < |h.elements| then [h.elements[currentLevel]] + getLevelHelper(h, targetLevel, currentLevel + 1)
    else []
  else getLevelHelper(h, targetLevel, currentLevel + 1)

{
  if n == 0 then 1
  else 2 * Power2(n - 1)
}

predicate {:spec} isMinHeap(h: Heap)
{
  forall i :: 0 < i < |h.elements| ==> h.elements[parent(i)] <= h.elements[i]
}

// Check max-heap property
predicate {:spec} isMaxHeap(h: Heap)
{
  forall i :: 0 < i < |h.elements| ==> h.elements[parent(i)] >= h.elements[i]
}

// Get minimum element (root of min-heap)
function {:spec} getMin(h: Heap): int
  requires !heapIsEmpty(h)
  requires isMinHeap(h)
{
  h.elements[0]
}

// Get maximum element (root of max-heap)
function {:spec} getMax(h: Heap): int
  requires !heapIsEmpty(h)
  requires isMaxHeap(h)
{
  h.elements[0]
}

// Check if element exists in heap
predicate {:spec} heapContains(h: Heap, x: int)
{
  x in h.elements
}

// Create empty heap
function {:spec} emptyHeap(): Heap
{
  Heap([])
}

// Create heap from single element
function {:spec} singletonHeap(x: int): Heap
{
  Heap([x])
}

// Swap two elements in sequence
function {:spec} swap(s: seq<int>, i: nat, j: nat): seq<int>
  requires i < |s| && j < |s|
{
  s[i := s[j]][j := s[i]]
}

// Check if heap is complete binary tree (always true for array representation)
predicate {:spec} isComplete(h: Heap)
{
  true  // Array representation is always complete
}

// Get height of heap
function {:spec} heapHeight(h: Heap): nat
{
  if |h.elements| == 0 then 0
  else log2Floor(|h.elements|) + 1
}

// Floor of log base 2
function {:spec} log2Floor(n: nat): nat
  requires n > 0
  decreases n
{
  if n == 1 then 0
  else 1 + log2Floor(n / 2)
}

// Check if index is valid
predicate {:spec} validIndex(h: Heap, i: nat)
{
  i < |h.elements|
}

// Get all elements at a given level
function {:spec} getLevel(h: Heap, level: nat): seq<int>
{
  getLevelHelper(h, level, 0)
}

function getLevelHelper(h: Heap, targetLevel: nat, currentLevel: nat): seq<int>
  decreases |h.elements| - currentLevel
{
  if currentLevel >= |h.elements| || currentLevel >= Power2(targetLevel) then []
  else if currentLevel >= Power2(targetLevel) - 1 && currentLevel < Power2(targetLevel + 1) - 1 then
    if currentLevel < |h.elements| then [h.elements[currentLevel]] + getLevelHelper(h, targetLevel, currentLevel + 1)
    else []
  else getLevelHelper(h, targetLevel, currentLevel + 1)
}

function Power2(n: nat): nat
{
  if n == 0 then 1
  else 2 * Power2(n - 1)
}

// --- Lemmas for correctness ---

lemma EmptyHeapIsMinHeap()
  ensures isMinHeap(emptyHeap())
{
  var h := emptyHeap();
  forall i | 0 < i < |h.elements|
    ensures h.elements[parent(i)] <= h.elements[i]
  {
    assert false;  // No such i exists
  }
}

lemma EmptyHeapIsMaxHeap()
  ensures isMaxHeap(emptyHeap())
{
  var h := emptyHeap();
  forall i | 0 < i < |h.elements|
    ensures h.elements[parent(i)] >= h.elements[i]
  {
    assert false;  // No such i exists
  }
}

lemma SingletonIsMinHeap(x: int)
  ensures isMinHeap(singletonHeap(x))
{
  var h := singletonHeap(x);
  forall i | 0 < i < |h.elements|
    ensures h.elements[parent(i)] <= h.elements[i]
  {
    assert false;  // No such i exists since |h.elements| == 1
  }
}

lemma SingletonIsMaxHeap(x: int)
  ensures isMaxHeap(singletonHeap(x))
{
  var h := singletonHeap(x);
  forall i | 0 < i < |h.elements|
    ensures h.elements[parent(i)] >= h.elements[i]
  {
    assert false;  // No such i exists since |h.elements| == 1
  }
}

lemma MinHeapRootIsMinimum(h: Heap)
  requires !heapIsEmpty(h)
  requires isMinHeap(h)
  ensures forall i :: 0 <= i < |h.elements| ==> h.elements[0] <= h.elements[i]
{
  if |h.elements| == 1 {
    forall i | 0 <= i < |h.elements|
      ensures h.elements[0] <= h.elements[i]
    {
      assert i == 0;
    }
  } else {
    forall i | 0 <= i < |h.elements|
      ensures h.elements[0] <= h.elements[i]
    {
      if i == 0 {
        // Trivial
      } else {
        MinHeapPathToRoot(h, i);
      }
    }
  }
}

lemma MinHeapPathToRoot(h: Heap, i: nat)
  requires isMinHeap(h)
  requires 0 < i < |h.elements|
  ensures h.elements[0] <= h.elements[i]
{
  if parent(i) == 0 {
    assert h.elements[0] <= h.elements[i];
  } else {
    assert h.elements[parent(i)] <= h.elements[i];
    MinHeapPathToRoot(h, parent(i));
  }
}

lemma MaxHeapRootIsMaximum(h: Heap)
  requires !heapIsEmpty(h)
  requires isMaxHeap(h)
  ensures forall i :: 0 <= i < |h.elements| ==> h.elements[0] >= h.elements[i]
{
  if |h.elements| == 1 {
    forall i | 0 <= i < |h.elements|
      ensures h.elements[0] >= h.elements[i]
    {
      assert i == 0;
    }
  } else {
    forall i | 0 <= i < |h.elements|
      ensures h.elements[0] >= h.elements[i]
    {
      if i == 0 {
        // Trivial
      } else {
        MaxHeapPathToRoot(h, i);
      }
    }
  }
}

lemma MaxHeapPathToRoot(h: Heap, i: nat)
  requires isMaxHeap(h)
  requires 0 < i < |h.elements|
  ensures h.elements[0] >= h.elements[i]
{
  if parent(i) == 0 {
    assert h.elements[0] >= h.elements[i];
  } else {
    assert h.elements[parent(i)] >= h.elements[i];
    MaxHeapPathToRoot(h, parent(i));
  }
}

lemma ParentChildRelation(i: nat)
  requires i > 0
  ensures leftChild(parent(i)) == i || rightChild(parent(i)) == i
  ensures leftChild(parent(i)) == i <==> i % 2 == 1
  ensures rightChild(parent(i)) == i <==> i % 2 == 0
{
  var p := parent(i);
  assert p == (i - 1) / 2;
  assert leftChild(p) == 2 * p + 1;
  assert rightChild(p) == 2 * p + 2;

  if i % 2 == 1 {
    assert i == 2 * ((i - 1) / 2) + 1;
    assert leftChild(p) == i;
  } else {
    assert i % 2 == 0;
    assert i == 2 * ((i - 1) / 2) + 2;
    assert rightChild(p) == i;
  }
}

lemma HeapHeightBound(h: Heap)
  ensures heapHeight(h) <= |h.elements|
{
if |h.elements| == 0 {
    assert heapHeight(h) == 0;
    assert 0 <= |h.elements|;
  } else {
    var n := |h.elements|;
    assert log2Floor(n) < n by Log2FloorBound(n);
    assert heapHeight(h) == log2Floor(n) + 1;
    assert log2Floor(n) + 1 <= n by {
      if n == 1 {
        assert log2Floor(1) + 1 == 0 + 1 == 1;
      } else {
        // For n > 1: log2Floor(n) + 1 <= n
        // Since log2Floor(n) < n (from Log2FloorBound), and both are integers,
        // we have log2Floor(n) + 1 <= n
        // More formally: log2Floor(n) <= n - 1, so log2Floor(n) + 1 <= n
        assert log2Floor(n) <= n - 1;
        assert log2Floor(n) + 1 <= n;
      }
    }
    assert heapHeight(h) <= |h.elements|;
  }
}

lemma Log2FloorBound(n: nat)
  requires n > 0
  ensures log2Floor(n) < n
  decreases n
{
  if n == 1 {
    assert log2Floor(1) == 0;
  } else {
    Log2FloorBound(n / 2);
    assert log2Floor(n) == 1 + log2Floor(n / 2);
    assert n / 2 < n;
  }
}

lemma SwapPreservesMultiset(s: seq<int>, i: nat, j: nat)
  requires i < |s| && j < |s|
  ensures multiset(swap(s, i, j)) == multiset(s)
{
  var s' := swap(s, i, j);
  assert s'[i] == s[j];
  assert s'[j] == s[i];
  forall k | 0 <= k < |s| && k != i && k != j
    ensures s'[k] == s[k]
  {
    // Elements other than i and j are unchanged
  }
}

// Min-heap operations: insert, extractMin, heapify with heap property

datatype Heap = Heap(elements: seq<int>)

// Check if heap is empty
predicate {:spec} heapIsEmpty(h: Heap)
{
  |h.elements| == 0
}

// Get heap size
function {:spec} heapSize(h: Heap): nat
{
  |h.elements|
}

// Parent index in heap
function {:spec} parent(i: nat): nat
  requires i > 0
{
  (i - 1) / 2
}

// Left child index
function {:spec} leftChild(i: nat): nat
{
  2 * i + 1
}

// Right child index
function {:spec} rightChild(i: nat): nat
{
  2 * i + 2
}

// Check min-heap property
predicate {:spec} isMinHeap(h: Heap)
{
  forall i :: 0 < i < |h.elements| ==> h.elements[parent(i)] <= h.elements[i]
}

// Check max-heap property
predicate {:spec} isMaxHeap(h: Heap)
{
  forall i :: 0 < i < |h.elements| ==> h.elements[parent(i)] >= h.elements[i]
}

// Get minimum element (root of min-heap)
function {:spec} getMin(h: Heap): int
  requires !heapIsEmpty(h)
  requires isMinHeap(h)
{
  h.elements[0]
}

// Get maximum element (root of max-heap)
function {:spec} getMax(h: Heap): int
  requires !heapIsEmpty(h)
  requires isMaxHeap(h)
{
  h.elements[0]
}

// Check if element exists in heap
predicate {:spec} heapContains(h: Heap, x: int)
{
  x in h.elements
}

// Create empty heap
function {:spec} emptyHeap(): Heap
{
  Heap([])
}

// Create heap from single element
function {:spec} singletonHeap(x: int): Heap
{
  Heap([x])
}

// Swap two elements in sequence
function {:spec} swap(s: seq<int>, i: nat, j: nat): seq<int>
  requires i < |s| && j < |s|
{
  s[i := s[j]][j := s[i]]
}

// Check if heap is complete binary tree (always true for array representation)
predicate {:spec} isComplete(h: Heap)
{
  true  // Array representation is always complete
}

// Get height of heap
function {:spec} heapHeight(h: Heap): nat
{
  if |h.elements| == 0 then 0
  else log2Floor(|h.elements|) + 1
}

// Floor of log base 2
function {:spec} log2Floor(n: nat): nat
  requires n > 0
  decreases n
{
  if n == 1 then 0
  else 1 + log2Floor(n / 2)
}

// Check if index is valid
predicate {:spec} validIndex(h: Heap, i: nat)
{
  i < |h.elements|
}

// Get all elements at a given level
function {:spec} getLevel(h: Heap, level: nat): seq<int>
{
  getLevelHelper(h, level, 0)
}

function getLevelHelper(h: Heap, targetLevel: nat, currentLevel: nat): seq<int>
  decreases |h.elements| - currentLevel
{
  if currentLevel >= |h.elements| || currentLevel >= Power2(targetLevel) then []
  else if currentLevel >= Power2(targetLevel) - 1 && currentLevel < Power2(targetLevel + 1) - 1 then
    if currentLevel < |h.elements| then [h.elements[currentLevel]] + getLevelHelper(h, targetLevel, currentLevel + 1)
    else []
  else getLevelHelper(h, targetLevel, currentLevel + 1)
}

function Power2(n: nat): nat
{
  if n == 0 then 1
  else 2 * Power2(n - 1)
}

lemma ParentChildRelation(i: nat)
  requires i > 0
  ensures leftChild(parent(i)) == i || rightChild(parent(i)) == i
  ensures leftChild(parent(i)) == i <==> i % 2 == 1
  ensures rightChild(parent(i)) == i <==> i % 2 == 0
{
  var p := parent(i);
  assert p == (i - 1) / 2;
  assert leftChild(p) == 2 * p + 1;
  assert rightChild(p) == 2 * p + 2;

  if i % 2 == 1 {
    assert i == 2 * ((i - 1) / 2) + 1;
    assert leftChild(p) == i;
  } else {
    assert i % 2 == 0;
    assert i == 2 * ((i - 1) / 2) + 2;
    assert rightChild(p) == i;
  }
}

lemma HeapHeightBound(h: Heap)
  ensures heapHeight(h) <= |h.elements|
{
if |h.elements| == 0 {
  assert heapHeight(h) == 0;
  assert 0 <= |h.elements|;
} else {
  var n := |h.elements|;
  assert log2Floor(n) < n by {
    Log2FloorBound(n);
  }
  assert heapHeight(h) == log2Floor(n) + 1;
  assert log2Floor(n) + 1 <= n by {
    if n == 1 {
      assert log2Floor(1) + 1 == 0 + 1 == 1;
    } else {
      assert log2Floor(n) <= n - 1;
      assert log2Floor(n) + 1 <= n;
    }
  }
  assert heapHeight(h) <= |h.elements|;
}
}

lemma Log2FloorBound(n: nat)
  requires n > 0
  ensures log2Floor(n) < n
  decreases n
{
  if n == 1 {
    assert log2Floor(1) == 0;
  } else {
    Log2FloorBound(n / 2);
    assert log2Floor(n) == 1 + log2Floor(n / 2);
    assert n / 2 < n;
  }
}

function sum(xs: seq<int>): int
{
  if |xs| == 0 then 0
  else xs[0] + sum(xs[1..])
}

function sumTail(xs: seq<int>, acc: int): int
  decreases |xs|
{
  if |xs| == 0 then acc
  else sumTail(xs[1..], acc + xs[0])
}

lemma sumCorrect(xs: seq<int>)
  ensures sum(xs) == sumTail(xs, 0)
{
  sumCorrectHelper(xs, 0);
}

lemma sumCorrectHelper(xs: seq<int>, acc: int)
  ensures sumTail(xs, acc) == acc + sum(xs)
{
  if |xs| == 0 {
  } else {
    calc {
      sumTail(xs, acc);
      == sumTail(xs[1..], acc + xs[0]);
      == { sumCorrectHelper(xs[1..], acc + xs[0]); }
      (acc + xs[0]) + sum(xs[1..]);
      == acc + (xs[0] + sum(xs[1..]));
      == acc + sum(xs);
    }
  }
}

lemma sumAppend(xs: seq<int>, ys: seq<int>)
  ensures sum(xs + ys) == sum(xs) + sum(ys)
{
  if |xs| == 0 {
    assert xs + ys == ys;
  } else {
    assert xs + ys == [xs[0]] + (xs[1..] + ys);
    calc {
      sum(xs + ys);
      == xs[0] + sum((xs[1..] + ys));
      == { sumAppend(xs[1..], ys); }
      xs[0] + (sum(xs[1..]) + sum(ys));
      == (xs[0] + sum(xs[1..])) + sum(ys);
      == sum(xs) + sum(ys);
    }
  }
}

  else sumTail(xs[1..], acc + xs[0])

{
  sumCorrectHelper(xs, 0);

lemma sumCorrectHelper(xs: seq<int>, acc: int)
  ensures sumTail(xs, acc) == acc + sum(xs)
{
  if |xs| == 0 {
  } else {
    calc {
      sumTail(xs, acc);
      == sumTail(xs[1..], acc + xs[0]);
      == { sumCorrectHelper(xs[1..], acc + xs[0]); }
      (acc + xs[0]) + sum(xs[1..]);
      == acc + (xs[0] + sum(xs[1..]));
      == acc + sum(xs);
    }
  }

lemma sumAppend(xs: seq<int>, ys: seq<int>)
  ensures sum(xs + ys) == sum(xs) + sum(ys)
{
  if |xs| == 0 {
    assert xs + ys == ys;
  } else {
    assert xs + ys == [xs[0]] + (xs[1..] + ys);
    calc {
      sum(xs + ys);
      == xs[0] + sum((xs[1..] + ys));
      == { sumAppend(xs[1..], ys); }
      xs[0] + (sum(xs[1..]) + sum(ys));
      == (xs[0] + sum(xs[1..])) + sum(ys);
      == sum(xs) + sum(ys);
    }
  }
}

lemma sumDistributive(xs: seq<int>, c: int)
  ensures sum(seq(|xs|, i requires 0 <= i < |xs| => c * xs[i])) == c * sum(xs)
{
if |xs| == 0 {
  } else {
    calc {
      sum(seq(|xs|, i requires 0 <= i < |xs| => c * xs[i]));
      == c * xs[0] + sum(seq(|xs| - 1, i requires 0 <= i < |xs| - 1 => c * xs[i + 1]));
      == { sumDistributive(xs[1..], c); }
      c * xs[0] + c * sum(xs[1..]);
      == c * (xs[0] + sum(xs[1..]));
      == c * sum(xs);
    }
  }
}

{
  if |xs| == 0 then 0
  else xs[0] + sum(xs[1..])
}

function sumTail(xs: seq<int>, acc: int): int
  decreases |xs|
{
  if |xs| == 0 then acc
  else sumTail(xs[1..], acc + xs[0])
}

lemma sumCorrect(xs: seq<int>)
  ensures sum(xs) == sumTail(xs, 0)
{
  sumCorrectHelper(xs, 0);
}

lemma sumCorrectHelper(xs: seq<int>, acc: int)
  ensures sumTail(xs, acc) == acc + sum(xs)
{
  if |xs| == 0 {
  } else {
    calc {
      sumTail(xs, acc);
      == sumTail(xs[1..], acc + xs[0]);
      == { sumCorrectHelper(xs[1..], acc + xs[0]); }
      (acc + xs[0]) + sum(xs[1..]);
      == acc + (xs[0] + sum(xs[1..]));
      == acc + sum(xs);
    }
  }
}

lemma sumAppend(xs: seq<int>, ys: seq<int>)
  ensures sum(xs + ys) == sum(xs) + sum(ys)
{
  if |xs| == 0 {
    assert xs + ys == ys;
  } else {
    assert xs + ys == [xs[0]] + (xs[1..] + ys);
    calc {
      sum(xs + ys);
      == xs[0] + sum((xs[1..] + ys));
      == { sumAppend(xs[1..], ys); }
      xs[0] + (sum(xs[1..]) + sum(ys));
      == (xs[0] + sum(xs[1..])) + sum(ys);
      == sum(xs) + sum(ys);
    }
  }
}

lemma sumDistributive(xs: seq<int>, c: int)
  ensures sum(seq(|xs|, i requires 0 <= i < |xs| => c * xs[i])) == c * sum(xs)
{
if |xs| == 0 {
  // Empty sequence case: both sides are 0
  assert seq(0, i => c * xs[i]) == [];
  assert sum([]) == 0;
  assert c * sum([]) == 0;
} else {
  // Non-empty sequence case
  // First, show that the sequence from 0 to |xs|-1 with step 1,
  // when sliced from index 1 onwards, equals the sequence for xs[1..]
  assert seq(|xs|, i requires 0 <= i < |xs| => c * xs[i])[1..] == seq(|xs| - 1, i requires 0 <= i < |xs| - 1 => c * xs[i + 1]);
  
  calc {
    sum(seq(|xs|, i requires 0 <= i < |xs| => c * xs[i]));
    == c * xs[0] + sum(seq(|xs|, i requires 0 <= i < |xs| => c * xs[i])[1..]);
    == { assert seq(|xs|, i requires 0 <= i < |xs| => c * xs[i])[1..] == seq(|xs| - 1, i requires 0 <= i < |xs| - 1 => c * xs[i + 1]); true; }
    c * xs[0] + sum(seq(|xs| - 1, i requires 0 <= i < |xs| - 1 => c * xs[i + 1]));
    == { sumDistributive(xs[1..], c); }
    c * xs[0] + c * sum(xs[1..]);
    == c * (xs[0] + sum(xs[1..]));
    == c * sum(xs);
  }
}
}

  assert seq(0, i => c * xs[i]) == [];

  assert c * sum([]) == 0;

  // Prove the key equality about the suffix of the constructed sequence
  assert seq(|xs|, i requires 0 <= i < |xs| => c * xs[i])[1..] ==
         seq(|xs| - 1, i requires 0 <= i < |xs| - 1 => c * xs[i + 1]);

    == c * (xs[0] + sum(xs[1..]));
    == c * sum(xs);

    // First, prove the head and tail of the new sequence
    var t := seq(|xs|, i requires 0 <= i < |xs| => c * xs[i]);
    assert t[0] == c * xs[0];
    assert t[1..] == seq(|xs|-1, i requires 0 <= i < |xs|-1 => c * xs[i+1]);

        // But to help Dafny, we explicitly state the arithmetic identity:
        assert c * xs[0] + c * sum(xs[1..]) == c * (xs[0] + sum(xs[1..]));
      }

// Finding maximum element in a sequence

predicate {:spec} isMax(s: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  m in s && forall x :: x in s ==> x <= m
}

function max(s: seq<int>): int
  requires |s| > 0
{
  if |s| == 1 then s[0]
  else 
    var restMax := max(s[1..]);
    if s[0] >= restMax then s[0] else restMax
}

lemma maxIsCorrect(s: seq<int>)
  requires |s| > 0
  ensures isMax(s, max(s))
{
if |s| == 1 {
  // Base case: s has exactly one element
  // Then max(s) == s[0], and we need to show s[0] in s && forall x :: x in s ==> x <= s[0]
  // The first part is trivial since s[0] is the only element
  // The second part: for the only element s[0], s[0] <= s[0] holds
  assert isMax(s, max(s));
} else {
  // Inductive step: |s| > 1
  // Let rest = s[1..], so |rest| > 0
  var rest := s[1..];
  // By inductive hypothesis (implicitly, via recursion), max(rest) is correct for rest
  // But we need to apply the lemma to rest, so we call it recursively
  maxIsCorrect(rest);
  // Now we know: isMax(rest, max(rest))
  // That is: max(rest) in rest && forall x :: x in rest ==> x <= max(rest)
  // Now max(s) = if s[0] >= max(rest) then s[0] else max(rest)
  // We need to show: max(s) in s && forall x :: x in s ==> x <= max(s)
  
  // First, show max(s) in s
  if s[0] >= max(rest) {
    // max(s) = s[0], and s[0] is in s by definition
    assert s[0] in s;
  } else {
    // max(s) = max(rest), and max(rest) in rest (by induction hypothesis)
    // and rest is a tail of s, so max(rest) in s
    assert max(rest) in rest;
    assert rest[..] in s; // rest elements are in s
    // Dafny knows: if x in rest and rest is a subsequence of s, then x in s
    assert max(rest) in s;
  }
  
  // Second, show forall x :: x in s ==> x <= max(s)
  // Any x in s is either s[0] or in rest
  // So we consider two cases:
  // 1. x = s[0]
  // 2. x in rest
  
  // Case 1: x = s[0]
  if s[0] >= max(rest) {
    // Then max(s) = s[0], so s[0] <= max(s) holds
    assert s[0] <= max(s);
  } else {
    // Then max(s) = max(rest), and we need s[0] <= max(rest)
    // But this case only happens when s[0] < max(rest), so it's true
    assert s[0] < max(rest) ==> s[0] <= max(rest);
    assert s[0] <= max(s);
  }
  
  // Case 2: x in rest
  // By induction hypothesis, x <= max(rest)
  // And max(rest) <= max(s) (since max(s) is either max(rest) or something >= max(rest))
  // So x <= max(s)
  // We can reason:
  //   if s[0] >= max(rest), then max(s) = s[0] >= max(rest), so x <= max(rest) <= max(s)
  //   else max(s) = max(rest), so x <= max(s) directly
  // Dafny can infer this with the two cases above
  
  // More precisely, we can split into the two cases again
  if s[0] >= max(rest) {
    // max(s) = s[0], and we know s[0] >= max(rest), so max(rest) <= max(s)
    // And by induction: x <= max(rest), so x <= max(s)
    assert max(rest) <= max(s);
  } else {
    // max(s) = max(rest), so x <= max(s) directly from induction
    assert max(rest) == max(s);
  }
  
  // Now combine: for all x in s, x <= max(s)
  // (This is implicit in the case analysis above, but we can rely on Dafny's reasoning)
}
}

// Finding maximum element in a sequence

predicate {:spec} isMax(s: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  m in s && forall x :: x in s ==> x <= m
}

function max(s: seq<int>): int
  requires |s| > 0
{
  if |s| == 1 then s[0]
  else 
    var restMax := max(s[1..]);
    if s[0] >= restMax then s[0] else restMax
}

lemma maxIsCorrect(s: seq<int>)
  requires |s| > 0
  ensures isMax(s, max(s))
{
if |s| == 1 {
  // Base case: s has exactly one element
  assert s[0] in s;
  assert forall x :: x in s ==> x <= s[0];
} else {
  // Inductive step: |s| > 1
  var rest := s[1..];
  maxIsCorrect(rest);
  
  // By induction: isMax(rest, max(rest))
  // i.e., max(rest) in rest && forall x :: x in rest ==> x <= max(rest)
  
  // Show max(s) in s
  if s[0] >= max(rest) {
    assert s[0] in s;
  } else {
    assert max(rest) in rest;
    // rest elements are in s (since rest = s[1..])
    assert forall i :: 0 <= i < |rest| ==> rest[i] in s;
    assert max(rest) in s;
  }
  
  // Show forall x :: x in s ==> x <= max(s)
  assert forall x :: x in s ==> x <= max(s) by {
    var x: int;
    if x in s {
      if x == s[0] {
        if s[0] >= max(rest) {
          assert s[0] == max(s);
        } else {
          assert s[0] < max(rest);
          assert max(s) == max(rest);
          assert s[0] <= max(rest);
        }
      } else {
        assert x in rest;
        assert x <= max(rest);
        if s[0] >= max(rest) {
          assert max(rest) <= s[0] == max(s);
        } else {
          assert max(rest) == max(s);
        }
        assert x <= max(s);
      }
    }
  }
}
}

  requires |s| > 0
  ensures isMax(s, max(s))
{

  assert s[0] in s;

} else {
  // Inductive step: |s| > 1
  var rest := s[1..];
  maxIsCorrect(rest);

  // i.e., max(rest) in rest && forall x :: x in rest ==> x <= max(rest)
  
  // Show max(s) in s
  if s[0] >= max(rest) {
    assert s[0] in s;
  } else {
    assert max(rest) in rest;
    // rest elements are in s (since rest = s[1..])
    assert forall i :: 0 <= i < |rest| ==> rest[i] in s;
    assert max(rest) in s;

          assert x <= max(rest);
          assert max(rest) <= s[0];

        } else {

          assert x <= max(rest);
          assert max(rest) == m;
          assert x <= m;
        }
      }

// Finding maximum element in a sequence

predicate {:spec} isMax(s: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  m in s && forall x :: x in s ==> x <= m
}

function max(s: seq<int>): int
  requires |s| > 0
{
  if |s| == 1 then s[0]
  else 
    var restMax := max(s[1..]);
    if s[0] >= restMax then s[0] else restMax
}

lemma maxIsCorrect(s: seq<int>)
  requires |s| > 0
  ensures isMax(s, max(s))
{
if |s| == 1 {
    // For singleton sequence, max(s) == s[0]
    // Need to show: s[0] in s && forall x :: x in s ==> x <= s[0]
    // Since |s| == 1, s == [s[0]], so:
    // 1. s[0] in s holds by definition
    // 2. For the only element s[0], s[0] <= s[0] holds
    // Dafny can prove this automatically
  } else {
    // For |s| > 1, let rest = s[1..], so |rest| > 0
    // By induction hypothesis, isMax(rest, max(rest))
    // max(s) = if s[0] >= max(rest) then s[0] else max(rest)
    
    // Let m_rest := max(rest), m := max(s)
    // By induction: isMax(rest, m_rest) holds
    // Case 1: s[0] >= m_rest, then m = s[0]
    //   Need: s[0] in s (true) and forall x :: x in s ==> x <= s[0]
    //   For x in rest: by IH, x <= m_rest <= s[0]
    //   For x = s[0]: s[0] <= s[0]
    // Case 2: s[0] < m_rest, then m = m_rest
    //   Need: m_rest in s and forall x :: x in s ==> x <= m_rest
    //   m_rest in rest ==> m_rest in s (true)
    //   For x in rest: x <= m_rest by IH
    //   For x = s[0]: s[0] < m_rest implies s[0] <= m_rest
    
    // Dafny can prove this automatically with induction
    // but we need to help it with the inductive hypothesis
    // We can call maxIsCorrect on the tail sequence
    var rest := s[1..];
    maxIsCorrect(rest);
    // Now we have isMax(rest, max(rest))
    // And by definition of max(s), we have the two cases
    // Dafny can complete the proof using these facts
  }
}
XP
// Finding maximum element in a sequence

predicate {:spec} isMax(s: seq<int>, m: int)
{
  m in s && forall x :: x in s ==> x <= m
}

function max(s: seq<int>): int
  requires |s| > 0
{
  if |s| == 1 then s[0]
  else 
    var restMax := max(s[1..]);
    if s[0] >= restMax then s[0] else restMax
}

lemma maxIsCorrect(s: seq<int>)
  requires |s| > 0
  ensures isMax(s, max(s))
{
if |s| == 1 {
  // For singleton sequence, max(s) == s[0]
  // Need to show: s[0] in s && forall x :: x in s ==> x <= s[0]
  // Since |s| == 1, s == [s[0]], so:
  // 1. s[0] in s holds by definition (element of sequence)
  // 2. For the only element s[0], s[0] <= s[0] holds by reflexivity
  // Dafny can prove this automatically with the following assertions for clarity
  assert s == [s[0]];
  assert s[0] in s;
  assert forall x :: x in s ==> x <= s[0];
} else {
  // For |s| > 1, consider rest = s[1..]
  var rest := s[1..];
  // By induction hypothesis, the max of rest is correct
  maxIsCorrect(rest);
  
  // Let m_rest := max(rest)
  // max(s) = if s[0] >= max(rest) then s[0] else max(rest)
  
  if s[0] >= max(rest) {
    // Case 1: max(s) = s[0]
    // Need to show: s[0] in s && forall x :: x in s ==> x <= s[0]
    
    // s[0] in s is true because s starts with s[0]
    assert s[0] in s;
    
    // For any element x in s:
    // Either x == s[0] (then x <= s[0] trivially), or x in rest
    // For x in rest: by IH, x <= max(rest) and max(rest) <= s[0] (since s[0] >= max(rest))
    assert forall x :: x in s ==> x <= s[0] by {
      var x;
      if x in s {
        if x == s[0] {
          assert x <= s[0];
        } else {
          // x in rest since s[0] is separate
          assert x in rest;
          // By IH: isMax(rest, max(rest)) so x <= max(rest)
          assert x <= max(rest);
          // By assumption: max(rest) <= s[0]
          assert max(rest) <= s[0];
          assert x <= s[0];
        }
      }
    };
  } else {
    // Case 2: max(s) = max(rest) (since s[0] < max(rest))
    // Need to show: max(rest) in s && forall x :: x in s ==> x <= max(rest)
    
    // max(rest) in rest and rest is a suffix of s, so max(rest) in s
    assert max(rest) in rest ==> max(rest) in s;
    assert max(rest) in rest by {
      // By IH: isMax(rest, max(rest)) so max(rest) in rest
      assert max(rest) in rest;
    };
    
    // For any element x in s:
    // Either x == s[0] (then x < max(rest) so x <= max(rest)), or x in rest
    // For x in rest: by IH, x <= max(rest)
    assert forall x :: x in s ==> x <= max(rest) by {
      var x;
      if x in s {
        if x == s[0] {
          assert s[0] < max(rest) by {
            // By assumption in this branch: s[0] < max(rest)
          };
          assert x <= max(rest);
        } else {
          // x in rest
          assert x in rest;
          // By IH: isMax(rest, max(rest)) so x <= max(rest)
          assert x <= max(rest);
        }
      }
    };
  }
}
}

          assert x <= max(rest);

datatype List<T> = Nil | Cons(head: T, tail: List<T>)

function reverse<T>(xs: List<T>): List<T>
{
  match xs
  case Nil => Nil
  case Cons(h, t) => append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil))
}

function append<T>(xs: List<T>, ys: List<T>): List<T>
{
  match xs
  case Nil => ys
  case Cons(h, t) => Cons(h, append(t, ys))
}

predicate {:spec} isPalindrome<T(==)>(xs: List<T>)
{
  xs == reverse(xs)
}

function makePalindrome<T>(xs: List<T>): List<T>
{
  append(xs, reverse(xs))
}

lemma appendNilRight<T>(xs: List<T>)
  ensures append(xs, Nil) == xs
{
  match xs
  case Nil => 
  case Cons(h, t) => appendNilRight(t);
}

lemma appendAssoc<T>(xs: List<T>, ys: List<T>, zs: List<T>)
  ensures append(append(xs, ys), zs) == append(xs, append(ys, zs))
{
  match xs
  case Nil =>
  case Cons(h, t) => appendAssoc(t, ys, zs);
}

lemma reverseAppend<T>(xs: List<T>, ys: List<T>)
  ensures reverse(append(xs, ys)) == append(reverse(ys), reverse(xs))
{

}

lemma reverseReverse<T>(xs: List<T>)
  ensures reverse(reverse(xs)) == xs
{
  match xs
  case Nil =>
  case Cons(h, t) =>
    reverseReverse(t);
    reverseAppend(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil));
    assert reverse(Cons(h, Nil)) == Cons(h, Nil);
}

lemma makePalindromeCorrect<T>(xs: List<T>)
  ensures isPalindrome(makePalindrome(xs))
{
  calc == {
    reverse(makePalindrome(xs));
    reverse(append(xs, reverse(xs)));
    { reverseAppend(xs, reverse(xs)); }
    append(reverse(reverse(xs)), reverse(xs));
    { reverseReverse(xs); }
    append(xs, reverse(xs));
    makePalindrome(xs);
  }
}

{

  case Nil => ys
  case Cons(h, t) => Cons(h, append(t, ys))

predicate {:spec} isPalindrome<T(==)>(xs: List<T>)
{
  xs == reverse(xs)
}

function makePalindrome<T>(xs: List<T>): List<T>
{

lemma appendNilRight<T>(xs: List<T>)
  ensures append(xs, Nil) == xs
{

  case Nil => 
  case Cons(h, t) => appendNilRight(t);

lemma appendAssoc<T>(xs: List<T>, ys: List<T>, zs: List<T>)
  ensures append(append(xs, ys), zs) == append(xs, append(ys, zs))
{
  match xs
  case Nil =>
  case Cons(h, t) => appendAssoc(t, ys, zs);

lemma reverseAppend<T>(xs: List<T>, ys: List<T>)
  ensures reverse(append(xs, ys)) == append(reverse(ys), reverse(xs))
{
match xs
case Nil =>
  // reverse(append(Nil, ys)) == reverse(ys)
  // append(reverse(ys), reverse(Nil)) == append(reverse(ys), Nil) == reverse(ys)
  // by appendNilRight(reverse(ys))
case Cons(h, t) =>
  // reverse(append(Cons(h, t), ys)) == reverse(Cons(h, append(t, ys))) 
  // == append(reverse(append(t, ys)), Cons(h, Nil))
  // by IH: reverse(append(t, ys)) == append(reverse(ys), reverse(t))
  // so: append(append(reverse(ys), reverse(t)), Cons(h, Nil))
  // == append(reverse(ys), append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil)))
  // == append(reverse(ys), reverse(Cons(h, t))) by definition of reverse
  reverseAppend(t, ys);
  // Now we need to show:
  // append(append(reverse(ys), reverse(t)), Cons(h, Nil)) == append(reverse(ys), append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil)))
  // This follows from associativity of append
  appendAssoc(reverse(ys), reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil));
  // Also need: reverse(Cons(h, t)) == append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil))
  // which is by definition of reverse and appendNilRight(Cons(h, Nil))
  assert reverse(Cons(h, t)) == append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil));
}

lemma reverseReverse<T>(xs: List<T>)
  ensures reverse(reverse(xs)) == xs
{
  match xs
  case Nil =>
  case Cons(h, t) =>
    reverseReverse(t);
    reverseAppend(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil));
    assert reverse(Cons(h, Nil)) == Cons(h, Nil);
}

    append(reverse(reverse(xs)), reverse(xs));
    { reverseReverse(xs); }
    append(xs, reverse(xs));
    makePalindrome(xs);
  }

lemma reverseAppend<T>(xs: List<T>, ys: List<T>)
  ensures reverse(append(xs, ys)) == append(reverse(ys), reverse(xs))
{
match xs
case Nil =>
  // reverse(append(Nil, ys)) == reverse(ys)
  // append(reverse(ys), reverse(Nil)) == append(reverse(ys), Nil) == reverse(ys)
  // by appendNilRight(reverse(ys))
  assert reverse(append(Nil, ys)) == reverse(ys) by {
    // append(Nil, ys) == ys
    // so reverse(append(Nil, ys)) == reverse(ys)
    // this follows from definition of append
  };
  assert reverse(Nil) == Nil;
  assert append(reverse(ys), reverse(Nil)) == append(reverse(ys), Nil);
  assert append(reverse(ys), Nil) == reverse(ys) by {
    appendNilRight(reverse(ys));
  };
case Cons(h, t) =>
  reverseAppend(t, ys);
  // reverse(append(Cons(h, t), ys)) == reverse(Cons(h, append(t, ys))) 
  // == append(reverse(append(t, ys)), Cons(h, Nil))
  // by IH: reverse(append(t, ys)) == append(reverse(ys), reverse(t))
  // so: append(append(reverse(ys), reverse(t)), Cons(h, Nil))
  // == append(reverse(ys), append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil)))
  // == append(reverse(ys), reverse(Cons(h, t))) by definition of reverse
  assert reverse(append(Cons(h, t), ys)) == append(reverse(append(t, ys)), Cons(h, Nil)) by {
    // reverse(Cons(h, append(t, ys))) == append(reverse(append(t, ys)), Cons(h, Nil))
    // by definition of reverse
  };
  assert reverse(append(t, ys)) == append(reverse(ys), reverse(t)) by {
    reverseAppend(t, ys);
  };
  assert append(reverse(append(t, ys)), Cons(h, Nil)) == append(append(reverse(ys), reverse(t)), Cons(h, Nil));
  assert append(append(reverse(ys), reverse(t)), Cons(h, Nil)) == append(reverse(ys), append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil))) by {
    appendAssoc(reverse(ys), reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil));
  };
  assert append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil)) == reverse(Cons(h, t)) by {
    // reverse(Cons(h, t)) == append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil))
    // by definition of reverse
  };
  assert append(reverse(ys), append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil))) == append(reverse(ys), reverse(Cons(h, t)));
}

lemma reverseAppend<T>(xs: List<T>, ys: List<T>)
  ensures reverse(append(xs, ys)) == append(reverse(ys), reverse(xs))
{
match xs
case Nil =>
  assert reverse(append(Nil, ys)) == reverse(ys) by {
    // append(Nil, ys) == ys by definition
    // so reverse(append(Nil, ys)) == reverse(ys)
  };
  assert reverse(Nil) == Nil;
  assert append(reverse(ys), reverse(Nil)) == append(reverse(ys), Nil) by {
    // reverse(Nil) == Nil
  };

    appendNilRight(reverse(ys));
  };
case Cons(h, t) =>
  reverseAppend(t, ys);
  assert reverse(append(Cons(h, t), ys)) == reverse(Cons(h, append(t, ys))) by {
    // by definition of append
  };
  assert reverse(Cons(h, append(t, ys))) == append(reverse(append(t, ys)), Cons(h, Nil)) by {
    // by definition of reverse
  };
  assert reverse(append(t, ys)) == append(reverse(ys), reverse(t)) by {
    reverseAppend(t, ys);
  };
  assert append(reverse(append(t, ys)), Cons(h, Nil)) == append(append(reverse(ys), reverse(t)), Cons(h, Nil)) by {
    // substitution
  };
  assert append(append(reverse(ys), reverse(t)), Cons(h, Nil)) == append(reverse(ys), append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil))) by {
    appendAssoc(reverse(ys), reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil));
  };
  assert append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil)) == reverse(Cons(h, t)) by {
    // by definition of reverse
  };
  assert append(reverse(ys), append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil))) == append(reverse(ys), reverse(Cons(h, t))) by {
    // substitution
  };
}

lemma appendAssoc<T>(xs: List<T>, ys: List<T>, zs: List<T>)
  ensures append(append(xs, ys), zs) == append(xs, append(ys, zs))

  match xs
  case Nil =>
  case Cons(h, t) => appendAssoc(t, ys, zs);

lemma reverseAppend<T>(xs: List<T>, ys: List<T>)
  ensures reverse(append(xs, ys)) == append(reverse(ys), reverse(xs))
{
match xs
case Nil =>
  // reverse(append(Nil, ys)) == reverse(ys)
  // reverse(append(ys, Nil)) == reverse(ys)  [by appendNilRight on ys, then reverse identity]
  // reverse(append(Nil, ys)) == append(reverse(ys), reverse(Nil))  [since reverse(Nil) == Nil]
  // Hence: reverse(ys) == append(reverse(ys), Nil)  [which holds by appendNilRight]
  appendNilRight(reverse(ys));
case Cons(h, t) =>
  // reverse(append(Cons(h, t), ys))
  // = reverse(Cons(h, append(t, ys)))
  // = append(reverse(append(t, ys)), Cons(h, Nil))
  // By IH: reverse(append(t, ys)) == append(reverse(ys), reverse(t))
  // So: append(append(reverse(ys), reverse(t)), Cons(h, Nil))
  // = append(reverse(ys), append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil)))
  // = append(reverse(ys), reverse(Cons(h, t)))  [since reverse(Cons(h, t)) = append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil))]
  reverseAppend(t, ys);
  appendAssoc(reverse(ys), reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil));
  reverseAppend(Cons(h, Nil), Nil); // to get reverse(Cons(h, Nil)) == Cons(h, Nil)
  // Actually, we need to show: append(reverse(ys), reverse(Cons(h, t))) == append(reverse(ys), append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil)))
  // But reverse(Cons(h, t)) == append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil)) is a known fact.
  // We can prove it separately, but here we just need to rewrite:
  // reverse(Cons(h, t)) == append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil))
  // This is definitional in our reverse function: reverse(Cons(h, t)) = append(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil))
  // So the result follows directly by congruence.
}

lemma reverseReverse<T>(xs: List<T>)
  ensures reverse(reverse(xs)) == xs
{
  match xs
  case Nil =>
  case Cons(h, t) =>
    reverseReverse(t);
    reverseAppend(reverse(t), Cons(h, Nil));
    assert reverse(Cons(h, Nil)) == Cons(h, Nil);
}
