  ensures a + (b + c) == (a + b) + c
{
  // Dafny proves this automatically
}

lemma QueueSizeProperty<T>(q: Queue<T>)
  ensures queueSize(q) == |queueToSeq(q)|
{
  ReverseLength(q.rear);
}

lemma EnqueueCorrect<T>(q: Queue<T>, x: T)
  ensures queueToSeq(enqueue(q, x)) == queueToSeq(q) + [x]
  ensures queueSize(enqueue(q, x)) == queueSize(q) + 1
{
  var q' := enqueue(q, x);
  assert q'.front == q.front;
  assert q'.rear == [x] + q.rear;

  ReverseAppend([x], q.rear);
  assert reverse([x]) == [x];
  assert reverse([x] + q.rear) == reverse(q.rear) + reverse([x]);
  assert reverse([x] + q.rear) == reverse(q.rear) + [x];

  calc == {
    queueToSeq(q');
    q'.front + reverse(q'.rear);
    q.front + reverse([x] + q.rear);
    q.front + (reverse(q.rear) + [x]);
    { SeqAssoc(q.front, reverse(q.rear), [x]); }
    (q.front + reverse(q.rear)) + [x];
    queueToSeq(q) + [x];
  }

  QueueSizeProperty(q);
  QueueSizeProperty(q');
}

lemma DequeueCorrect<T>(q: Queue<T>)
  requires !queueIsEmpty(q)
  ensures |queueToSeq(q)| > 0
  ensures queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == queueToSeq(q)[1..]
  ensures queueFront(q) == queueToSeq(q)[0]
{
// First, ensure queueToSeq(q) is non-empty
assert |queueToSeq(q)| > 0 by {
  // Since q is not empty, queueSize(q) > 0
  assert queueSize(q) > 0 by {
    // q is not empty, so either front or rear is non-empty
    if q.front != [] || q.rear != [] {
      assert |q.front| + |q.rear| > 0;
    }
  }
  // Using QueueSizeProperty: queueSize(q) == |queueToSeq(q)|
  assert |queueToSeq(q)| == queueSize(q) > 0;
}

// Handle two cases: front non-empty vs front empty
if |q.front| > 0 {
  // Case 1: front non-empty
  var q' := dequeue(q);
  assert q'.front == q.front[1..];
  assert q'.rear == q.rear;
  
  // Prove queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == queueToSeq(q)[1..]
  calc == {
    queueToSeq(q');
    q'.front + reverse(q'.rear);
    q.front[1..] + reverse(q.rear);
    // Since q.front is non-empty, (q.front + reverse(q.rear))[1..] == q.front[1..] + reverse(q.rear)
    { assert (q.front + reverse(q.rear))[1..] == q.front[1..] + reverse(q.rear) by {
        // This follows from sequence slicing: for non-empty s1, (s1 + s2)[1..] == s1[1..] + s2
        if |q.front| == 1 {
          assert (q.front + reverse(q.rear))[1..] == reverse(q.rear);
          assert q.front[1..] == [];
        } else {
          // s1 has length >= 2
          assert (q.front + reverse(q.rear))[1..] == q.front[1..] + reverse(q.rear);
        }
      }
    }
    queueToSeq(q)[1..];
  }
  
  // Prove queueFront(q) == queueToSeq(q)[0]
  assert queueFront(q) == q.front[0];
  assert queueToSeq(q)[0] == (q.front + reverse(q.rear))[0] == q.front[0];
} else {
  // Case 2: front is empty => rear must be non-empty (since queue not empty)
  assert |q.rear| > 0;
  
  // Handle sub-cases for dequeue
  if |q.rear| == 1 {
    // Sub-case: rear has exactly one element
    var q' := dequeue(q);
    assert q'.front == [];
    assert q'.rear == [];
    
    // queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == []
    assert queueToSeq(q') == [];
    
    // queueToSeq(q) == reverse(q.rear) == [q.rear[|q.rear|-1]] = [q.rear[0]]
    // So queueToSeq(q)[1..] == []
    assert queueToSeq(q) == reverse(q.rear);
    assert reverse(q.rear) == [q.rear[0]] by {
      ReverseLength(q.rear);
      if |q.rear| == 1 {
        assert reverse(q.rear) == [q.rear[0]];
      } else {
        // Not possible in this branch
        assert false;
      }
    }
    assert queueToSeq(q)[1..] == [];
    
    // queueFront(q) == q.rear[|q.rear|-1] == q.rear[0]
    // queueToSeq(q)[0] == reverse(q.rear)[0] == q.rear[|q.rear|-1] == q.rear[0]
    assert queueFront(q) == q.rear[|q.rear|-1];
    assert reverse(q.rear)[0] == q.rear[|q.rear|-1] by {
      ReverseFirst(q.rear);
    }
  } else {
    // Sub-case: rear has more than one element
    var q' := dequeue(q);
    assert q'.front == reverse(q.rear)[1..];
    assert q'.rear == [];
    
    // Prove queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == queueToSeq(q)[1..]
    calc == {
      queueToSeq(q');
      q'.front + reverse(q'.rear);
      reverse(q.rear)[1..] + reverse([]);
      reverse(q.rear)[1..] + [];
      reverse(q.rear)[1..];
      // queueToSeq(q) == reverse(q.rear), so queueToSeq(q)[1..] == reverse(q.rear)[1..]
      { assert queueToSeq(q) == reverse(q.rear); }
      queueToSeq(q)[1..];
    }
    
    // Prove queueFront(q) == queueToSeq(q)[0]
    assert queueFront(q) == q.rear[|q.rear|-1];
    assert queueToSeq(q)[0] == reverse(q.rear)[0];
    assert reverse(q.rear)[0] == q.rear[|q.rear|-1] by {
      ReverseFirst(q.rear);
    }
  }
}
}

lemma SimpleQueueEquivalence<T>(sq: SimpleQueue<T>, q: Queue<T>)
  requires sq.elements == queueToSeq(q)
  ensures simpleQueueIsEmpty(sq) == queueIsEmpty(q)
  ensures simpleQueueSize(sq) == queueSize(q)
{
  if queueIsEmpty(q) {
    assert q.front == [] && q.rear == [];
    assert queueToSeq(q) == [];
    assert sq.elements == [];
  }
  QueueSizeProperty(q);
}
XP
// Queue operations: enqueue, dequeue, isEmpty, size

datatype Queue<T> = Queue(front: seq<T>, rear: seq<T>)

function {:spec} queueEmpty<T>(): Queue<T>
{
  Queue([], [])
}

predicate {:spec} queueIsEmpty<T>(q: Queue<T>)
{
  q.front == [] && q.rear == []
}

function {:spec} enqueue<T>(q: Queue<T>, x: T): Queue<T>
{
  Queue(q.front, [x] + q.rear)
}

function {:spec} dequeue<T>(q: Queue<T>): Queue<T>
  requires !queueIsEmpty(q)
{
  if |q.front| > 0 then
    Queue(q.front[1..], q.rear)
  else
    // Front is empty, so we reverse rear and put it in front
    if |q.rear| == 1 then
      Queue([], [])
    else
      Queue(reverse(q.rear)[1..], [])
}

function {:spec} queueFront<T>(q: Queue<T>): T
  requires !queueIsEmpty(q)
{
  if |q.front| > 0 then
    q.front[0]
  else
    // Front is empty, so the front element is the first element of rear (when reversed)
    q.rear[|q.rear| - 1]
}

function {:spec} queueSize<T>(q: Queue<T>): nat
{
  |q.front| + |q.rear|
}

function {:spec} queueToSeq<T>(q: Queue<T>): seq<T>
{
  q.front + reverse(q.rear)
}

function reverse<T>(s: seq<T>): seq<T>
{
  if |s| == 0 then []
  else reverse(s[1..]) + [s[0]]
}

// Alternative queue representation with invariant
datatype SimpleQueue<T> = SimpleQueue(elements: seq<T>)

function {:spec} simpleQueueEmpty<T>(): SimpleQueue<T>
{
  SimpleQueue([])
}

predicate {:spec} simpleQueueIsEmpty<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>)
{
  q.elements == []
}

function {:spec} simpleEnqueue<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>, x: T): SimpleQueue<T>
{
  SimpleQueue(q.elements + [x])
}

function {:spec} simpleDequeue<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>): SimpleQueue<T>
  requires !simpleQueueIsEmpty(q)
{
  SimpleQueue(q.elements[1..])
}

function {:spec} simpleQueueFront<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>): T
  requires !simpleQueueIsEmpty(q)
{
  q.elements[0]
}

function {:spec} simpleQueueSize<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>): nat
{
  |q.elements|
}

lemma ReverseLength<T>(s: seq<T>)
  ensures |reverse(s)| == |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    // Base case
  } else {
    ReverseLength(s[1..]);
    assert |reverse(s)| == |reverse(s[1..])| + 1;
  }
}

lemma ReverseReverse<T>(s: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(reverse(s)) == s
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    // Base case
  } else {
    ReverseReverse(s[1..]);
    ReverseAppend(reverse(s[1..]), [s[0]]);
    assert reverse(reverse(s)) == s;
  }
}

lemma ReverseAppend<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1)
{
  if |s1| == 0 {
    assert s1 + s2 == s2;
    assert reverse(s1) == [];
  } else {
    assert s1 + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
    ReverseAppend(s1[1..], s2);
  }
}

lemma ReverseFirst<T>(s: seq<T>)
  requires |s| > 0
  ensures |reverse(s)| == |s|
  ensures reverse(s)[|reverse(s)| - 1] == s[0]
  ensures reverse(s)[0] == s[|s| - 1]
{
  ReverseLength(s);
  if |s| == 1 {
    assert reverse(s) == [s[0]];
  } else {
    ReverseFirst(s[1..]);
    assert reverse(s) == reverse(s[1..]) + [s[0]];
    ReverseLength(s[1..]);
    assert |reverse(s[1..])| == |s| - 1;
  }
}

lemma SeqAssoc<T>(a: seq<T>, b: seq<T>, c: seq<T>)
  ensures a + (b + c) == (a + b) + c
{
  // Dafny proves this automatically
}

lemma QueueSizeProperty<T>(q: Queue<T>)
  ensures queueSize(q) == |queueToSeq(q)|
{
  ReverseLength(q.rear);
}

lemma EnqueueCorrect<T>(q: Queue<T>, x: T)
  ensures queueToSeq(enqueue(q, x)) == queueToSeq(q) + [x]
  ensures queueSize(enqueue(q, x)) == queueSize(q) + 1
{
  var q' := enqueue(q, x);
  assert q'.front == q.front;
  assert q'.rear == [x] + q.rear;

  ReverseAppend([x], q.rear);
  assert reverse([x]) == [x];
  assert reverse([x] + q.rear) == reverse(q.rear) + reverse([x]);
  assert reverse([x] + q.rear) == reverse(q.rear) + [x];

  calc == {
    queueToSeq(q');
    q'.front + reverse(q'.rear);
    q.front + reverse([x] + q.rear);
    q.front + (reverse(q.rear) + [x]);
    { SeqAssoc(q.front, reverse(q.rear), [x]); }
    (q.front + reverse(q.rear)) + [x];
    queueToSeq(q) + [x];
  }

  QueueSizeProperty(q);
  QueueSizeProperty(q');
}

lemma DequeueCorrect<T>(q: Queue<T>)
  requires !queueIsEmpty(q)
  ensures |queueToSeq(q)| > 0
  ensures queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == queueToSeq(q)[1..]
  ensures queueFront(q) == queueToSeq(q)[0]
{
// First, ensure queueToSeq(q) is non-empty
assert |queueToSeq(q)| > 0 by {
  // Since q is not empty, at least one of front or rear is non-empty
  if q.front != [] || q.rear != [] {
    // Use QueueSizeProperty: |queueToSeq(q)| == queueSize(q)
    assert |queueToSeq(q)| == queueSize(q) by {
      QueueSizeProperty(q);
    }
    // queueSize(q) = |front| + |rear| > 0 since q is not empty
    assert queueSize(q) > 0;
    assert |queueToSeq(q)| > 0;
  }
}

// Handle two cases: front non-empty vs front empty
if |q.front| > 0 {
  // Case 1: front non-empty
  var q' := dequeue(q);
  assert q'.front == q.front[1..];
  assert q'.rear == q.rear;
  
  // Prove queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == queueToSeq(q)[1..]
  calc == {
    queueToSeq(q');
    q'.front + reverse(q'.rear);
    q.front[1..] + reverse(q.rear);
    // Key insight: for s1 non-empty, (s1 + s2)[1..] == s1[1..] + s2
    { 
      assert (q.front + reverse(q.rear))[1..] == q.front[1..] + reverse(q.rear) by {
        SeqAssoc(q.front[0..1], q.front[1..], reverse(q.rear));
        assert q.front == q.front[0..1] + q.front[1..];
        // Dafny knows sequence slicing properties
      }
    }
    (q.front + reverse(q.rear))[1..];
    queueToSeq(q)[1..];
  }
  
  // Prove queueFront(q) == queueToSeq(q)[0]
  assert queueFront(q) == q.front[0];
  assert queueToSeq(q)[0] == (q.front + reverse(q.rear))[0] == q.front[0] by {
    assert |q.front| > 0;
    assert (q.front + reverse(q.rear))[0] == q.front[0];
  }
} else {
  // Case 2: front is empty => rear must be non-empty (since queue not empty)
  assert |q.rear| > 0 by {
    if q.rear == [] {
      assert q.front == [] && q.rear == [];
      assert queueIsEmpty(q);
      assert false;
    }
  }
  
  // Handle sub-cases for dequeue
  if |q.rear| == 1 {
    // Sub-case: rear has exactly one element
    var q' := dequeue(q);
    assert q'.front == [];
    assert q'.rear == [];
    
    // queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == []
    assert queueToSeq(q') == [];
    
    // queueToSeq(q) == reverse(q.rear) == [q.rear[0]] (since |q.rear| == 1)
    assert queueToSeq(q) == reverse(q.rear) == [q.rear[0]] by {
      ReverseLength(q.rear);
      if |q.rear| == 1 {
        assert reverse(q.rear) == [q.rear[0]];
      }
    }
    assert queueToSeq(q)[1..] == [];
    
    // queueFront(q) == q.rear[0] (since |q.rear| == 1)
    assert queueFront(q) == q.rear[|q.rear|-1] == q.rear[0];
    assert queueToSeq(q)[0] == reverse(q.rear)[0] == q.rear[|q.rear|-1] == q.rear[0] by {
      ReverseFirst(q.rear);
    }
  } else {
    // Sub-case: rear has more than one element
    var q' := dequeue(q);
    assert q'.front == reverse(q.rear)[1..];
    assert q'.rear == [];
    
    // Prove queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == queueToSeq(q)[1..]
    calc == {
      queueToSeq(q');
      q'.front + reverse(q'.rear);
      reverse(q.rear)[1..] + reverse([]);
      reverse(q.rear)[1..] + [];
      reverse(q.rear)[1..];
      { assert queueToSeq(q) == reverse(q.rear); }
      queueToSeq(q)[1..];
    }
    
    // Prove queueFront(q) == queueToSeq(q)[0]
    assert queueFront(q) == q.rear[|q.rear|-1];
    assert queueToSeq(q)[0] == reverse(q.rear)[0];
    assert reverse(q.rear)[0] == q.rear[|q.rear|-1] by {
      ReverseFirst(q.rear);
    }
  }
}
}

lemma SimpleQueueEquivalence<T>(sq: SimpleQueue<T>, q: Queue<T>)
  requires sq.elements == queueToSeq(q)
  ensures simpleQueueIsEmpty(sq) == queueIsEmpty(q)
  ensures simpleQueueSize(sq) == queueSize(q)
{
  if queueIsEmpty(q) {
    assert q.front == [] && q.rear == [];
    assert queueToSeq(q) == [];
    assert sq.elements == [];
  }
  QueueSizeProperty(q);

lemma ReverseAppend<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1)
{
  if |s1| == 0 {
    assert s1 + s2 == s2;
    assert reverse(s1) == [];
  } else {
    assert s1 + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
    ReverseAppend(s1[1..], s2);
  }

  requires |s| > 0
  ensures |reverse(s)| == |s|
  ensures reverse(s)[|reverse(s)| - 1] == s[0]
  ensures reverse(s)[0] == s[|s| - 1]

  ReverseLength(s);
  if |s| == 1 {
    assert reverse(s) == [s[0]];
  } else {
    ReverseFirst(s[1..]);
    assert reverse(s) == reverse(s[1..]) + [s[0]];
    ReverseLength(s[1..]);
    assert |reverse(s[1..])| == |s| - 1;
  }
}

function reverse<T>(s: seq<T>): seq<T>
{
  if |s| == 0 then []
  else reverse(s[1..]) + [s[0]]
}

// Alternative queue representation with invariant
datatype SimpleQueue<T> = SimpleQueue(elements: seq<T>)

function {:spec} simpleQueueEmpty<T>(): SimpleQueue<T>
{
  SimpleQueue([])
}

predicate {:spec} simpleQueueIsEmpty<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>)
{
  q.elements == []
}

function {:spec} simpleEnqueue<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>, x: T): SimpleQueue<T>
{
  SimpleQueue(q.elements + [x])
}

function {:spec} simpleDequeue<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>): SimpleQueue<T>
  requires !simpleQueueIsEmpty(q)
{
  SimpleQueue(q.elements[1..])
}

function {:spec} simpleQueueFront<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>): T
  requires !simpleQueueIsEmpty(q)
{
  q.elements[0]
}

function {:spec} simpleQueueSize<T>(q: SimpleQueue<T>): nat
{
  |q.elements|
}

lemma ReverseLength<T>(s: seq<T>)
  ensures |reverse(s)| == |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    // Base case
  } else {
    ReverseLength(s[1..]);
    assert |reverse(s)| == |reverse(s[1..])| + 1;
  }
}

lemma ReverseReverse<T>(s: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(reverse(s)) == s
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    // Base case
  } else {
    ReverseReverse(s[1..]);
    ReverseAppend(reverse(s[1..]), [s[0]]);
    assert reverse(reverse(s)) == s;
  }
}

lemma ReverseAppend<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1)
{
  if |s1| == 0 {
    assert s1 + s2 == s2;
    assert reverse(s1) == [];
  } else {
    assert s1 + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
    ReverseAppend(s1[1..], s2);
  }
}

lemma ReverseFirst<T>(s: seq<T>)
  requires |s| > 0
  ensures |reverse(s)| == |s|
  ensures reverse(s)[|reverse(s)| - 1] == s[0]
  ensures reverse(s)[0] == s[|s| - 1]
{
  ReverseLength(s);
  if |s| == 1 {
    assert reverse(s) == [s[0]];
  } else {
    ReverseFirst(s[1..]);
    assert reverse(s) == reverse(s[1..]) + [s[0]];
    ReverseLength(s[1..]);
    assert |reverse(s[1..])| == |s| - 1;
  }
}

lemma SeqAssoc<T>(a: seq<T>, b: seq<T>, c: seq<T>)
  ensures a + (b + c) == (a + b) + c
{
  // Dafny proves this automatically
}

lemma QueueSizeProperty<T>(q: Queue<T>)
  ensures queueSize(q) == |queueToSeq(q)|
{
  ReverseLength(q.rear);
}

lemma EnqueueCorrect<T>(q: Queue<T>, x: T)
  ensures queueToSeq(enqueue(q, x)) == queueToSeq(q) + [x]
  ensures queueSize(enqueue(q, x)) == queueSize(q) + 1
{
  var q' := enqueue(q, x);
  assert q'.front == q.front;
  assert q'.rear == [x] + q.rear;

  ReverseAppend([x], q.rear);
  assert reverse([x]) == [x];
  assert reverse([x] + q.rear) == reverse(q.rear) + reverse([x]);
  assert reverse([x] + q.rear) == reverse(q.rear) + [x];

  calc == {
    queueToSeq(q');
    q'.front + reverse(q'.rear);
    q.front + reverse([x] + q.rear);
    q.front + (reverse(q.rear) + [x]);
    { SeqAssoc(q.front, reverse(q.rear), [x]); }
    (q.front + reverse(q.rear)) + [x];
    queueToSeq(q) + [x];
  }

  QueueSizeProperty(q);
  QueueSizeProperty(q');
}

lemma DequeueCorrect<T>(q: Queue<T>)
  requires !queueIsEmpty(q)
  ensures |queueToSeq(q)| > 0
  ensures queueToSeq(dequeue(q)) == queueToSeq(q)[1..]
  ensures queueFront(q) == queueToSeq(q)[0]
{
if |q.front| > 0 {
  // Front is non-empty: dequeue just removes the first element
  var q' := dequeue(q);
  assert q'.front == q.front[1..];
  assert q'.rear == q.rear;
  
  // Show queueToSeq(q')[1..] == queueToSeq(q)[1..]
  calc == {
    queueToSeq(q');
    q'.front + reverse(q'.rear);
    q.front[1..] + reverse(q.rear);
    { SeqAssoc(q.front[1..], reverse(q.rear), []); }
    (q.front + reverse(q.rear))[1..];
    queueToSeq(q)[1..];
  }
  
  // Show queueFront(q) == queueToSeq(q)[0]
  assert queueFront(q) == q.front[0];
  assert queueToSeq(q)[0] == (q.front + reverse(q.rear))[0] == q.front[0];
} else {
  // Front is empty, so we reverse rear and put it in front
  assert |q.rear| > 0 by {
    // Since queue is not empty and front is empty, rear must be non-empty
    assert !(q.front == [] && q.rear == []);
    assert q.front == [];
    assert q.rear != [];
  }
  
  // Handle the dequeue when front is empty
  var q' := dequeue(q);
  assert q'.front == reverse(q.rear)[1..];
  assert q'.rear == [];
  
  // Show queueToSeq(q')[1..] == queueToSeq(q)[1..]
  calc == {
    queueToSeq(q');
    q'.front + reverse(q'.rear);
    reverse(q.rear)[1..] + reverse([]);
    reverse(q.rear)[1..] + [];
    reverse(q.rear)[1..];
    { ReverseFirst(q.rear); }
    (q.front + reverse(q.rear))[1..];
    queueToSeq(q)[1..];
  }
  
  // Show queueFront(q) == queueToSeq(q)[0]
  assert queueFront(q) == q.rear[|q.rear| - 1];
  assert queueToSeq(q) == q.front + reverse(q.rear) == reverse(q.rear);
  assert reverse(q.rear)[0] == q.rear[|q.rear| - 1] by {
    ReverseFirst(q.rear);
  }
  assert queueToSeq(q)[0] == q.rear[|q.rear| - 1];
}
}

lemma SimpleQueueEquivalence<T>(sq: SimpleQueue<T>, q: Queue<T>)
  requires sq.elements == queueToSeq(q)
  ensures simpleQueueIsEmpty(sq) == queueIsEmpty(q)
  ensures simpleQueueSize(sq) == queueSize(q)
{
  if queueIsEmpty(q) {
    assert q.front == [] && q.rear == [];
    assert queueToSeq(q) == [];
    assert sq.elements == [];
  }
  QueueSizeProperty(q);
}

lemma reverse_permutes<T>(l: seq<T>)
  ensures forall x :: x in l <==> x in reverse(l)
{
  if |l| == 0 {
  } else {
    reverse_permutes(l[1..]);
    forall x
      ensures x in l <==> x in reverse(l)
    {
      if x == l[0] {
        assert x in reverse(l);
      } else {
        assert x in l <==> x in l[1..];
        assert x in l[1..] <==> x in reverse(l[1..]);
        assert x in reverse(l[1..]) ==> x in reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]];
      }
    }
  }
}

  ensures reverse(reverse(l)) == l
{

    calc {
      reverse(reverse(l));
      == reverse(reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]);
      == { reverse_append(reverse(l[1..]), [l[0]]); }
      reverse([l[0]]) + reverse(reverse(l[1..]));
      == [l[0]] + reverse(reverse(l[1..]));
      == { reverse_involutes(l[1..]); }
      [l[0]] + l[1..];
      == l;
    }
  }
}

lemma reverse_append<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1)
{
if |s1| == 0 {
  calc {
    reverse([] + s2);
    == reverse(s2);
    == reverse(s2) + [];
    == reverse(s2) + reverse([]);
  }
} else {
  reverse_append(s1[1..], s2);
  calc {
    reverse(s1 + s2);
    == reverse([s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2));
    == reverse((s1[1..] + s2) + [s1[0]]);
    == reverse([s1[0]]) + reverse(s1[1..] + s2);
    == [s1[0]] + (reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..]));
    == reverse(s2) + ([s1[0]] + reverse(s1[1..]));
    == reverse(s2) + reverse([s1[0]] + s1[1..]);
    == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1);
  }
}
}

lemma reverse_involutes<T>(l: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(reverse(l)) == l
{
  if |l| == 0 {
  } else {
    calc {
      reverse(reverse(l));
      == reverse(reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]);
      == { reverse_append(reverse(l[1..]), [l[0]]); }
      reverse([l[0]]) + reverse(reverse(l[1..]));
      == [l[0]] + reverse(reverse(l[1..]));
      == { reverse_involutes(l[1..]); }
      [l[0]] + l[1..];
      == l;
    }
  }
}

lemma reverse_append<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1)
{
if |s1| == 0 {
  calc {
    reverse([] + s2);
    == reverse(s2);
    == reverse(s2) + [];
    == reverse(s2) + reverse([]);
  }
} else {
  reverse_append(s1[1..], s2);
  reverse_permutes([s1[0]]);
  reverse_permutes(s1[1..] + s2);
  reverse_permutes(s1);
  calc {
    reverse(s1 + s2);
    == reverse([s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2));
    == reverse(s1[1..] + s2 + [s1[0]]);
    == { reverse_append(s1[1..] + s2, [s1[0]]); }
      reverse([s1[0]]) + reverse(s1[1..] + s2);
    == [s1[0]] + (reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..]));
    == reverse(s2) + ([s1[0]] + reverse(s1[1..]));
    == reverse(s2) + reverse([s1[0]]) + reverse(s1[1..]);
    == reverse(s2) + reverse([s1[0]] + s1[1..]);
    == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1);
  }
}
}

lemma reverse_append<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1)
{
if |s1| == 0 {
    assert s1 + s2 == s2;
    assert reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2);
    assert reverse(s1) == [];
    assert reverse(s2) + reverse(s1) == reverse(s2) + [];
    assert reverse(s2) + [] == reverse(s2);
  } else {
    reverse_append(s1[1..], s2);
    calc {
      reverse(s1 + s2);
      == reverse([s1[0]] + s1[1..] + s2);
      == reverse((s1[1..] + s2) + [s1[0]]);  // by seq associativity
      == reverse([s1[0]]) + reverse(s1[1..] + s2);  // by reverse_append with swapped args (or by expanding def)
      == [s1[0]] + (reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..]));  // by IH and reverse_append([s1[0]], s2) not needed—use reverse_append(s1[1..], s2)
      == [s1[0]] + reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..]);
      == reverse(s2) + [s1[0]] + reverse(s1[1..]);  // reassociate
      == reverse(s2) + (reverse([s1[0]]) + reverse(s1[1..]));
      == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..] + [s1[0]]);  // reverse_append(s1[1..], [s1[0]]) — but simpler:
      == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1);  // since s1 == [s1[0]] + s1[1..], so reverse(s1) = reverse([s1[0]] + s1[1..]) = reverse(s1[1..]) + [s1[0]], but we already have [s1[0]] + reverse(s1[1..]) == reverse(s1)
    }
  }
}

lemma reverse_involutes<T>(l: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(reverse(l)) == l
{
  if |l| == 0 {
  } else {
    calc {
      reverse(reverse(l));
      == reverse(reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]);
      == { reverse_append(reverse(l[1..]), [l[0]]); }
      reverse([l[0]]) + reverse(reverse(l[1..]));
      == [l[0]] + reverse(reverse(l[1..]));
      == { reverse_involutes(l[1..]); }
      [l[0]] + l[1..];
      == l;
    }
  }
}

      ensures x in l <==> x in reverse(l)

      } else {

lemma reverse_append<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1)
{
if |s1| == 0 {
    assert s1 + s2 == s2;
    assert reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2);
    assert reverse(s1) == [];
    assert reverse(s2) + reverse(s1) == reverse(s2) + [];
    assert reverse(s2) + [] == reverse(s2);
  } else {
    reverse_append(s1[1..], s2);
    reverse_permutes(s1[1..]);
    reverse_permutes(s2);
    assert s1 == [s1[0]] + s1[1..];
    assert s1 + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
    assert reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse([s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2));
    assert reverse([s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2)) == reverse(s1[1..] + s2) + [s1[0]];
    assert reverse(s1[1..] + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..]) by {
      reverse_append(s1[1..], s2);
    }
    assert reverse(s1 + s2) == (reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..])) + [s1[0]];
    assert reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..]) + [s1[0]] == reverse(s2) + (reverse(s1[1..]) + [s1[0]]);
    assert reverse(s1[1..]) + [s1[0]] == reverse(s1) by {
      assert s1 == [s1[0]] + s1[1..];
      assert reverse([s1[0]] + s1[1..]) == reverse(s1[1..]) + [s1[0]];
      reverse_append([s1[0]], s1[1..]);
    }
    assert reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1);
  }
}

lemma reverse_involutes<T>(l: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(reverse(l)) == l
{
  if |l| == 0 {
  } else {
    calc {
      reverse(reverse(l));
      == reverse(reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]);
      == { reverse_append(reverse(l[1..]), [l[0]]); }
      reverse([l[0]]) + reverse(reverse(l[1..]));
      == [l[0]] + reverse(reverse(l[1..]));
      == { reverse_involutes(l[1..]); }
      [l[0]] + l[1..];
      == l;
    }
  }
}

lemma reverse_append<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1)
{
decreases |s1|
{
  if |s1| == 0 {
    assert s1 + s2 == s2;
    assert reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2);
    assert reverse(s1) == [];
    assert reverse(s2) + reverse(s1) == reverse(s2) + [];
    assert reverse(s2) + [] == reverse(s2);
  } else {
    reverse_append(s1[1..], s2);
    assert s1 == [s1[0]] + s1[1..];
    assert s1 + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
    assert reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse([s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2));
    assert reverse([s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2)) == reverse(s1[1..] + s2) + [s1[0]];
    assert reverse(s1[1..] + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..]);
    assert reverse(s1 + s2) == (reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..])) + [s1[0]];
    assert reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..]) + [s1[0]] == reverse(s2) + (reverse(s1[1..]) + [s1[0]]);
    assert reverse(s1[1..]) + [s1[0]] == reverse(s1) by {
      reverse_append([s1[0]], s1[1..]);
    }
    assert reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1);
  }
}
}

    assert reverse(s1) == [];
    assert reverse(s2) + [] == reverse(s2);
  } else {
    assert s1 == [s1[0]] + s1[1..];
    assert s1 + s2 == ([s1[0]] + s1[1..]) + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
    
    calc {
      reverse(s1 + s2);
      == reverse([s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2));
      == reverse((s1[1..] + s2)) + [s1[0]];
      == { reverse_append(s1[1..], s2); }
      (reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..])) + [s1[0]];
      == { assert (reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..])) + [s1[0]] == 
           reverse(s2) + (reverse(s1[1..]) + [s1[0]]); }

      == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1);

lemma reverse_involutes<T>(l: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(reverse(l)) == l
{
reverse_permutes(l);
reverse(reverse(l)) == l
{
  // First, we know reverse(l) permutes l (from reverse_permutes)
  // But we need to show double reversal gives original sequence
  // Use induction: assume reverse(reverse(l[1..])) == l[1..]
  reverse_involutes(l[1..]);
  
  // We need: reverse(reverse(l)) == l
  // Compute reverse(l) = reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]
  // So reverse(reverse(l)) = reverse(reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]])
  // Use reverse_append: reverse(a + b) = reverse(b) + reverse(a)
  reverse_append(reverse(l[1..]), [l[0]]);
  
  // Now: reverse(reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]) == reverse([l[0]]) + reverse(reverse(l[1..]))
  // reverse([l[0]]) == [l[0]] (can be shown separately or as known property)
  // and reverse(reverse(l[1..])) == l[1..] (by induction hypothesis)
  // So: [l[0]] + l[1..] == l (since l == [l[0]] + l[1..])
  
  // Prove reverse([x]) == [x] for any x
  // (We can include this as a local lemma or derive it)
  // For singleton: reverse([l[0]]) == reverse([] + [l[0]]) == reverse([l[0]]) + reverse([]) == reverse([l[0]]) + []
  // Actually better: by definition: reverse([l[0]]) == reverse([]) + [l[0]] == [] + [l[0]] == [l[0]]
  
  // Now apply calc:
  calc {
    reverse(reverse(l));
    == reverse(reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]);  // by definition of reverse
    == reverse([l[0]]) + reverse(reverse(l[1..]));  // by reverse_append
    == [l[0]] + reverse(reverse(l[1..]));  // since reverse([l[0]]) == [l[0]]
    == [l[0]] + l[1..];                    // by induction hypothesis
    == l;                                  // by definition of l
  }
}
}
XP

  else reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]
}

lemma reverse_involutes<T>(l: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(reverse(l)) == l
{
if |l| == 0 {
    assert reverse(l) == [];
    assert reverse(reverse(l)) == reverse([]);
    assert reverse([]) == [];
    assert reverse(reverse(l)) == l;
  } else {
    reverse_involutes(l[1..]);
    reverse_append(reverse(l[1..]), [l[0]]);
    calc {
      reverse(reverse(l));
      == reverse(reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]);  // by definition of reverse
      == reverse([l[0]]) + reverse(reverse(l[1..]));  // by reverse_append
      == [l[0]] + reverse(reverse(l[1..]));  // by reverse_single (reverse([x]) == [x])
      == [l[0]] + l[1..];                    // by induction hypothesis
      == l;                                  // by definition of l
    }
  }
}
XP
function reverse<T>(l: seq<T>): seq<T>
{
  if |l| == 0 then []
  else reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]
}

lemma reverse_permutes<T>(l: seq<T>)
  ensures forall x :: x in l <==> x in reverse(l)
{
  if |l| == 0 {
  } else {
    reverse_permutes(l[1..]);
    forall x
      ensures x in l <==> x in reverse(l)
    {
      if x == l[0] {
        assert x in reverse(l);
      } else {
        assert x in l <==> x in l[1..];
        assert x in l[1..] <==> x in reverse(l[1..]);
        assert x in reverse(l[1..]) ==> x in reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]];
      }
    }
  }
}

lemma reverse_append<T>(s1: seq<T>, s2: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(s1 + s2) == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1)
{
  if |s1| == 0 {
    assert s1 + s2 == s2;
    assert reverse(s1) == [];
    assert reverse(s2) + [] == reverse(s2);
  } else {
    assert s1 == [s1[0]] + s1[1..];
    assert s1 + s2 == ([s1[0]] + s1[1..]) + s2 == [s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2);
    
    calc {
      reverse(s1 + s2);
      == reverse([s1[0]] + (s1[1..] + s2));
      == reverse((s1[1..] + s2)) + [s1[0]];
      == { reverse_append(s1[1..], s2); }
      (reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..])) + [s1[0]];
      == { assert (reverse(s2) + reverse(s1[1..])) + [s1[0]] == 
           reverse(s2) + (reverse(s1[1..]) + [s1[0]]); }
      reverse(s2) + (reverse(s1[1..]) + [s1[0]]);
      == reverse(s2) + reverse(s1);
    }
  }
}

lemma reverse_involutes<T>(l: seq<T>)
  ensures reverse(reverse(l)) == l
{
if |l| == 0 {
  assert reverse(l) == [];
  assert reverse(reverse(l)) == reverse([]);
  reverse<T>([]);
  assert reverse(reverse(l)) == l;
} else {
  reverse_involutes(l[1..]);
  reverse_append(reverse(l[1..]), [l[0]]);
  calc {
    reverse(reverse(l));
    == reverse(reverse(l[1..]) + [l[0]]);  // by definition of reverse
    == reverse([l[0]]) + reverse(reverse(l[1..]));  // by reverse_append
    == [l[0]] + reverse(reverse(l[1..]));  // by reverse_single
    == [l[0]] + l[1..];                    // by induction hypothesis
    == l;                                  // by definition of l
  }
}
